{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 07:59:39","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 07:59:39","title":"How to Create a Family Portrait Photoshop Action","link":"https://design.tutsplus.com/tutorials/how-to-create-a-family-portrait-photoshop-action--cms-35405","description":"<figure class=\"final-product final-product--image\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/final_image/final-product.jpg\" alt=\"Final product image\"><!--googleoff: index--><figcaption>What You'll Be Creating</figcaption><!--googleon: index--></figure><p>In this family portrait Photoshop tutorial, you'll learn how to create a family portrait Photoshop action. I will explain everything in so much detail that everyone can follow it, even those who have just opened Photoshop for the first time.</p><h2>What You Will Learn in This Family Portrait Actions Photoshop Tutorial<br>\n</h2><ul>\n<li>How to make Photoshop actions<br>\n</li>\n<li>How to edit family portraits in Photoshop</li>\n<li>How to do a good family portrait filter in Photoshop</li>\n<li>How to make adjustments<br>\n</li>\n<li>How to save a family portrait action in Photoshop<br>\n</li>\n</ul><h2>What You'll Need</h2><p>To recreate the design above, you will need the following resources:</p><ul><li>\n<a href=\"https://www.twenty20.com/photos/4d18f5c2-c7ea-4ff1-9ceb-ef67fcb3256f\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Stock Image</a>\n</li></ul><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">1.</span> How to Get Started<br>\n</h2><p>First, open the photo that you want to work with. To open your photo, go to <strong>File &gt; Open</strong>, choose your photo, and click <strong>Open</strong>. Now, before we get started, just check a couple of things:</p><ol>\n<li>Your photo should be in <strong>RGB Color</strong> mode, <strong>8 Bits/Channel</strong>. To check this, go to <strong>Image &gt; Mode</strong>.</li>\n<li>For best results, your photo size should be <strong>2000–4000 px wide/high</strong>. To check this, go to<strong> Image &gt; Image Size</strong>.</li>\n<li>Your photo should be the <strong>Background</strong> layer. If it is not, go to <strong>Layer &gt; New &gt; Background from Layer</strong>.</li>\n</ol><p>I've both resized and cropped the image.<br></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"checking image mode and size\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/checking-image-mode-and-size.jpg\"></figure><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">2.</span> How to Start Recording a Family Portrait Photoshop Action<br>\n</h2><p>In this section, we are going to start recording the Photoshop family portrait action. Go to <strong>Window &gt; Actions</strong>, and in the <strong>Actions</strong> panel, click on the menu icon in the top right-hand corner, choose <strong>New Set</strong> to create a new set, and name it <strong>Family Portrait</strong>. Then, click on the same menu icon again, choose <strong>New Action</strong> to create a new action, and name it <strong>Family Portrait</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating new Photoshop action\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/creating-new-Photoshop-action.jpg\"></figure><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">3.</span> How to Do a Good Family Portrait Filter in Photoshop</h2><h3>Step 1</h3><p>In this section, we are going to do some photo retouching using a combination of different Photoshop filters. Press <strong>Control-J</strong> on your keyboard to duplicate the <strong>Background </strong>layer. Then,  go to <strong>Image &gt; Auto Tone</strong>, <strong>Image &gt; Auto Contrast</strong>, and <strong>Image &gt; Auto Color</strong> to make some auto-corrections to the layer tone, contrast, and color.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"making auto adjustments\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/making-auto-adjustments.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 2</h3><p>Now go to <strong>Image &gt; Adjustments &gt; Shadows/Highlights</strong>, and set <strong>Shadows</strong> to <strong>10%</strong> and <strong>Highlights</strong> to<strong> 0%</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adjusting shadows and highlights\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/adjusting-shadows-and-highlights.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 3</h3><p>Go to <strong>Filter &gt; Noise &gt; Reduce Noise</strong> and set the <strong>Strength</strong> to <strong>10</strong>, <strong>Preserve Details</strong> to <strong>25%</strong>, <strong>Reduce Color Noise</strong> to<strong> 50%</strong>, and <strong>Sharpen Details</strong> to<strong> 25%</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adding reduce noise filter\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/adding-reduce-noise-filter.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 4</h3><p>Now go to <strong>Filter &gt; Blur &gt; Surface Blur</strong>, and set the <strong>Radius</strong> to<strong> 5 px</strong> and <strong>Threshold</strong> to<strong> 15</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adding surface blur filter\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/adding-surface-blur-filter.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 5</h3><p>Go to <strong>Filter &gt; Sharpen &gt; Unsharp Mask</strong>, and set the <strong>Amount</strong> to <strong>100%</strong>, <strong>Radius</strong> to <strong>2 px</strong>, and <strong>Threshold</strong> to <strong>0 levels</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adding unsharp mask filter\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/adding-unsharp-mask-filter.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 6</h3><p>Now go to <strong>Filter &gt; Blur &gt; Smart Blur</strong>, and set the <strong>Radius</strong> to<strong> 1</strong>, <strong>Threshold</strong> to <strong>50</strong>, <strong>Quality</strong> to <strong>High</strong>, and <strong>Mode</strong> to <strong>Normal</strong>.<br></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adding smart blur filter\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/adding-smart-blur-filter.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 7</h3><p>Go to <strong>Filter &gt; Sharpen &gt; Unsharp Mask</strong>, and set the <strong>Amount</strong> to <strong>50%</strong>, <strong>Radius</strong> to <strong>2 px</strong>, and <strong>Threshold</strong> to <strong>0 levels</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adding unsharp mask filter\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/adding-unsharp-mask-filter-2.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 8</h3><p>Now name this layer <strong>Retouching</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"renaming layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/renaming-layer.jpg\"></figure><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">4.</span> How to Edit Family Portraits in Photoshop With Adjustments<br>\n</h2><h3>Step 1</h3><p>In this section, we are going to make adjustments to our Photoshop family portrait action. Go to <strong>Layer &gt; New Adjustment Layer &gt; Curves</strong> to create a new curves adjustment layer and name it <strong>Color Look</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating new curves adjustment layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/creating-new-curves-adjustment-layer.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 2</h3><p>Now <strong>Double-click</strong> on this layer thumbnail and, in the <strong>Properties</strong> panel, enter the settings below:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adjusting curves\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/adjusting-curves.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 3</h3><p>Press <strong>D</strong> on your keyboard to reset the swatches. Then, go to <strong>Layer &gt; New Adjustment Layer &gt; Gradient Map</strong> to create a new gradient map adjustment layer and name it <strong>Overall Contrast</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating new gradient map adjustment layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/creating-new-gradient-map-adjustment-layer.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 4</h3><p>Now change the <strong>Blending Mode</strong> of this layer to <strong>Soft Light</strong> and set the <strong>Opacity </strong>to<strong> 30%</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"changing blending mode and opacity\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/changing-blending-mode-and-opacity.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 5</h3><p>Go to <strong>Layer &gt; New Adjustment Layer &gt; Curves</strong> to create a new curves adjustment layer, and name it <strong>Overall Brightness</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating new levels adjustment layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/creating-new-levels-adjustment-layer.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 6</h3><p>Now <strong>Double-click</strong> on this layer thumbnail and, in the <strong>Properties</strong> panel, enter the settings below:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adjusting levels\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/adjusting-levels.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 7</h3><p>Go to <strong>Layer &gt; New Adjustment Layer &gt; Vibrance</strong> to create a new vibrance adjustment layer and name it <strong>Overall Vibrance/Saturation</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating new vibrance adjustment layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/creating-new-vibrance-adjustment-layer.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 8</h3><p>Now <strong>Double-click</strong> on this layer thumbnail and, in the<strong> Properties</strong> panel, set the <strong>Vibrance</strong> to <strong>+20</strong> and the <strong>Saturation</strong> to <strong>+10</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adjusting vibrance and saturation\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/adjusting-vibrance-and-saturation.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 9</h3><p>Press <strong>Control-Alt-Shift-E</strong> on your keyboard to make a screenshot. Then, go to <strong>Filter &gt; Camera Raw Filter</strong> and enter the settings below:<strong><br></strong></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adding camera raw filter\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/adding-camera-raw-filter-2.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 10</h3><p>Now name this layer <strong>Final Adjustments</strong>. Then, go to <strong>Window &gt; Actions</strong>, and in the <strong>Actions</strong>\n panel, click on the rectangle icon  in the bottom left-hand corner to \nstop recording the action. Then, in the same panel, click on the menu \nicon in the top right-hand corner and choose<strong> Save Actions</strong> to save the action. <br></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"saving photoshop action\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/saving-photoshop-action.jpg\"></figure><h2>You Made It!</h2><p>Congratulations, you have \nsucceeded! You've learned how to create Photoshop actions for family portraits and how to edit a family portrait in Photoshop. Here is our \nfinal result:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"final result\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/final-result.jpg\"></figure><h2>Additional Results<br>\n</h2><p>Here are some additional results that I've made using the family portrait actions Photoshop tool we have just created:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"family portrait photoshop action\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/family-portrait-photoshop-action-2.jpg\"></figure><h2>5 Best Photoshop Actions for Family Portraits</h2><p>Want to see the best Photoshop actions for family portraits? Check out this list of family portrait Photoshop actions and presets from <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/add-ons/actions-and-presets\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Envato Elements</a>. Enjoy incredible filters, from Photoshop actions to Lightroom presets and more!</p><h3>\n<a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/lensdust-photoshop-action-AK7PA52\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">LensDust Photoshop Action</a> (ATN)</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/lensdust-photoshop-action-AK7PA52\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"lens dust photoshop action\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/lens-dust-photoshop-action.jpg\"></a></figure><p>Create these amazing lens dust effects from your \nfamily portrait photos with just a few clicks! Simply open your photo, brush over your \nsubject, choose the shape of the sparkles, and play the action. It’s really that \nsimple! Creating an advanced Photoshop lens dust effect has never been this easy and fun.</p><h3>\n<a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/double-exposure-action-Z5YMHL\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Double Exposure Photoshop Action</a> (ATN)</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/double-exposure-action-Z5YMHL\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"double exposure photoshop action\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/double-exposure-photoshop-action.jpg\"></a></figure><p>This action set includes four Photoshop actions to simulate a double exposure effect. You can combine these actions with any other actions as they aren't modifying the photo's colors.<br></p><h3>\n<a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/bouquet-wedding-actions-for-photoshop-GT92HG\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Bouquet Wedding Actions for Photoshop</a> (ATN)</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/bouquet-wedding-actions-for-photoshop-GT92HG\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"bouquet wedding actions for photoshop\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/bouquet-wedding-actions-for-photoshop.jpg\"></a></figure><p>The Bouquet Wedding collection features beautiful photo actions for weddings, engagements, and portrait photography.\nEnhance your Photoshop post-processing and create your signature artistic style!</p><h3>\n<a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/fingerprint-cs4-photoshop-action-BST428G\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Fingerprint Photoshop Action</a> (ATN, ABR, TXT)</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/fingerprint-cs4-photoshop-action-BST428G\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"fingerprint photoshop action\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/fingerprint-photoshop-action.jpg\"></a></figure><p>The Fingerprint Photoshop action was created in order to make a cool \nfingerprint effect from your photo. Use it to give an \ninteresting effect to simple photos, collages, backgrounds, etc. Just open your picture, brush over your object, and play the \naction.</p><h3>\n<a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/insta-blog-photoshop-actions-65LPNE\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Insta Blog Photoshop Actions</a> (ATN)</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/insta-blog-photoshop-actions-65LPNE\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"insta blog photoshop actions\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35405/image/insta-blog-photoshop-actions.jpg\"></a></figure><p>Insta Blog is a beautiful \ncollection specially hand-crafted for bloggers. It will create certain \ntones and styles within your images. This action works in a \nnon-destructive way to achieve a high-quality look. Moreover, the \noriginal image layer will remain unchanged. <br></p><p>Liked this family portrait Photoshop tutorial and learned how to edit a family portrait in Photoshop? The template is well organized in layers and is fully editable in InDesign. </p><h3>5. <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/product-catalog-bundle-no-1/8344222\" target=\"_self\">Product Catalog Bundle No 1</a> (INDD) </h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/product-catalog-bundle-no-1/8344222\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Product Catalog Bundle No 1\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/988/posts/34206/image/Product-Catalog-Template%20(5).jpg\"></a></figure><p>This beautiful item catalog template comes in three professional styles. Fully editable in InDesign, the template comes in A4 and US Letter. All you need to do in InDesign is to drop your own images into the placeholders. Type your text and change the colours and logos as you need. </p><h3>6. <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/interiors-brochure/5225137\" target=\"_self\">Interiors Brochure</a> (INDD, PSD)</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/interiors-brochure/5225137\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Interiors Brochure\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/988/posts/34206/image/Product-Catalog-Template%20(6).jpg\"></a></figure><p>This 24-page catalogue book template was designed specifically for interior designers, but it can be adapted to any industry.</p><p>The InDesign and Photoshop files come in A4 size only. The images, text, and backgrounds are separated on different layers, making them super easy to customise. If you get stuck, there's a help file included to help you out. </p><h3>7. <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/product-catalog-williams/8280732\" target=\"_self\">Product Catalog - Williams</a> (INDD)</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/product-catalog-williams/8280732\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Product Catalog - Williams\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/988/posts/34206/image/Product-Catalog-Template%20(7).jpg\"></a></figure><p> This is a professional and modern 16-page product catalogue template that can be customised to work with any business. The entire catalogue is easily edited and customised in InDesign. </p><p>Just drop in your own pictures and text, change your colours, add your logo, and your catalogue is ready to send to the printers. </p><h3>8. <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/horizontal-brochure-a5-audio-life/7818468\" target=\"_self\">Horizontal Brochure A5 Audio Life</a> (INDD)</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/horizontal-brochure-a5-audio-life/7818468\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Horizontal Brochure A5 Audio Life\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/988/posts/34206/image/Product-Catalog-Template%20(8).jpg\"></a></figure><p>For those looking for something a bit different, there's this ever so cool A5 product catalogue template. With just 16 pages, the template is one of the smaller catalogues found at GraphicRiver. Like all the other templates featured here, customisation is easy and fast. </p><h3>9. <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/product-catalog/3237321\" target=\"_self\">Product Catalog</a> (INDD)</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/product-catalog/3237321\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Product Catalog\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/988/posts/34206/image/Product-Catalog-Template%20(9).jpg\"></a></figure><p>This A4 template is made up of 16 page layouts, ready for you to customise as needed. The files are all well organised and layered in InDesign. So you can drop in your images easily, change the text and colours, and have your document ready for the printers in no time. </p><h3>10. <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/car-part-product-catalog-automobile-brochure/6537319\" target=\"_self\">Car Part Product Catalog - Automobile Brochure</a> (INDD)</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/car-part-product-catalog-automobile-brochure/6537319\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Car Part Product Catalog - Automobile Brochure\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/988/posts/34206/image/Product-Catalog-Template%20(10).jpg\"></a></figure><p>Looking for a catalogue that's designed specifically for promoting car parts? Then you need to see this item catalog template. The A4 template features a 12-page layout. It's organised in several layers to make editing easy, and like all the other templates here, this one is print ready. </p><h3>11. <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/product-catalog/11630273\" target=\"_self\">Product Catalog</a> (INDD)</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/product-catalog/11630273\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Product Catalog\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/988/posts/34206/image/Product-Catalog-Template%20(11).jpg\"></a></figure><p>When you want your products to shine, choose this A4 print-ready catalogue. It features 16 pages in A4 size. Simply add your own images and text, change the colours to match your brand or taste, and your project is ready to send to the printers. </p><h3>12. <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/fashion-lookbook-001/11062782\" target=\"_self\">Fashion Lookbook 001</a> (INDD)</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/fashion-lookbook-001/11062782\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Fashion Lookbook 001\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/988/posts/34206/image/Product-Catalog-Template%20(12).jpg\"></a></figure><p>Sometimes you're looking for a product catalog template in Word. For those times, there's this 34-page template with its clean and professional design. The template comes in A4 and US Letter paper size in light and dark versions. </p><p>The files are well organised in layers, and the structured pages use a document grid and a baseline grid for better positioning of elements.</p><h3>13. <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/fashion-lookbook/9299427\" target=\"_self\">Fashion Lookbook</a> (INDD)</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/fashion-lookbook/9299427\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Fashion Lookbook\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/988/posts/34206/image/Product-Catalog-Template%20(13).jpg\"></a></figure><p>This is a template designed with the fashion industry in mind. It comes in the form of a lookbook style for designers who want to show off their looks for the season. The template offers 24 pages in both A4 and US Letter size. The files are organised with images, text, and background on separate layers for easy customisation.</p><h3>14. <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/products-showcase-catalogue/549868\" target=\"_self\">Products Showcase Catalogue</a> (INDD)</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/products-showcase-catalogue/549868\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Products Showcase Catalogue\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/988/posts/34206/image/Product-Catalog-Template%20(14).jpg\"></a></figure><p>Here's another A5 template that's easily customisable for a variety of uses. The 16-page template offers a good variety of layouts. It offers A4 and US Letter InDesign catalog templates, as well as A4 and US Letter product catalogue PDF templates.</p><p>As with the other templates here, just drop in your own images and text, and change the colours. The template is ready for printing.</p><h2>5 Quick Tips for Product Catalogue Designs </h2><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/jasmine-lookbook-brochure-catalogue-5T3CAF\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"JASMINE- Lookbook Brochure Catalogue\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/34206/image/JASMINE%20copy.jpg\"></a></figure><p>If you want to know how to design a product catalog, you need to understand that designing a multi-page catalogue from scratch is an enormous undertaking. It requires a huge amount of time and an in-depth knowledge of programs like InDesign. </p><p>This is why we recommend product catalogue templates in this article. They not only offer you a wide variety of layout options, but also save you hours of work.</p><p>But whether you're making your own catalogue from scratch or using an online template,  there are a few things that you should keep in mind. Here are some of those things:  </p><h3>1. Select Your Design Software</h3><p> If you decide to create your catalogue from scratch on your own, you'll need a software package like InDesign to help you design your catalogue layout. </p><h3>2. Gather the Info That Goes Into Your Catalogue</h3><p>Here's some of the information you'll need:</p><ul>\n<li>product information</li>\n<li>images</li>\n</ul><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/art-gallery-exhibition-catalog-DELEY7\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Art Gallery Exhibition Catalog\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/34206/image/Screenshot%202019-11-13%20at%203.59.50%20am%20copy.jpg\"></a></figure><h3>3. Plan Your Catalogue Layout</h3><p>At this point, you need to think about how to organise both the product information and images. At a minimum, your catalogue will need:</p><ul>\n<li>a front and back cover</li>\n<li>introduction pages</li>\n<li>master pages: header, footer, thumb index, category colour, page columns, etc.</li>\n<li>table of contents</li>\n<li>chapter separators</li>\n<li>product layouts </li>\n</ul><h3>4. Proof Your Catalogue</h3><p>The next step is to carefully proof your catalogue for mistakes and typos. This is really important at this stage because once you go to print, any mistakes are there to stay.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/fashion-catalog-3QNL8D\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Fashion Catalog\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/34206/image/Screenshot%202019-11-13%20at%204.00.06%20am%20copy.jpg\"></a></figure><h3>5. Print Your Catalogue</h3><p>Once your catalogue is ready to be printed, decide how many copies you need and what paper quality you'd like. All these decisions affect the cost of printing your catalogue, so discuss them with your printer. </p><p>To learn more about making product catalogues from scratch, check out the following article:</p><ul class=\"roundup-block__contents posts--half-width roundup-block--list\"><li class=\"roundup-block__content\"><a class=\"roundup-block__content-link\" href=\"https://design.tutsplus.com/tutorials/how-to-make-an-indesign-catalog-template--cms-32836\"><img class=\"roundup-block__preview-image\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/32836/preview_image/Preview-image.jpg\"><div class=\"roundup-block__primary-category topic-design\">Adobe InDesign</div>\n<div class=\"roundup-block__content-title\">How to Make an InDesign Catalog Template</div>\n<div class=\"roundup-block__author\">Grace Fussell</div></a></li></ul><h2>Discover More Awesome Catalog and Brochure Templates</h2><p>I hope you've enjoyed the selection of the best product catalog templates we've got in Envato Elements and GraphicRiver. 07:59:39","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 07:59:39","title":"How to Make a Rap Album Cover Art (Using an Album Cover Maker)","link":"https://design.tutsplus.com/tutorials/how-to-make-a-rap-album-cover-art-using-an-album-cover-maker--cms-32969","description":"<p><img alt=\"Rap album cover art created with Placeit\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32969/image/rap-album-covers_1.jpg\"><br></p><p>If you’re an aspiring rap artist, independent rap label, or an MC spitting lyrics, at some point you’re going to need a cool album cover design to promote your work. <br></p><p>The <a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/?f_devices=Album%20Cover%20Maker&amp;h=42\">Placeit album cover maker app</a> offers a wide selection of album covers that you can customise in a matter of minutes to create amazing rap album covers. This album cover art maker is so simple to use that it doesn’t matter whether or not you have any graphic design experience. I’ll show you what I mean. </p><p>Follow along with us over on our <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/user/TutsPremium\" target=\"_self\">Envato Tuts+ YouTube channel</a>:</p><figure data-video-embed=\"true\" data-original-url=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=m1e_8PDNnGI\" class=\"embedded-video\">\n  <iframe src=\"//www.youtube.com/embed/m1e_8PDNnGI?rel=0\" frameborder=\"0\" webkitallowfullscreen=\"webkitallowfullscreen\" mozallowfullscreen=\"mozallowfullscreen\" allowfullscreen=\"allowfullscreen\"></iframe>\n</figure><h2><b>How to Make Rap Album Cover Art Using the Placeit Album Cover Maker</b></h2><h3><b>Step 1</b></h3><p>Navigate to <a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/?f_devices=Album%20Cover%20Maker&amp;h=42\">Placeit</a> and sign up for FREE! Then click on <strong>Designs</strong> in the header menu. Select <strong>Album Cover Maker</strong> in the sub-menu.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/?f_devices=Album%20Cover%20Maker&amp;h=42\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Placeit \" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32969/image/album-cover-maker_1.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Go to <a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/?f_devices=Album%20Cover%20Maker&amp;h=42\" target=\"_self\">Placeit</a> &gt; Designs &gt; Album Cover Maker</figcaption></figure><h3><b>Step 2</b></h3><p>Now you have two choices: Either type rap album cover in the search bar and narrow your search to the album covers designated for rap, or browse the entire catalogue of cool album covers, select the design you like the most, and use the customisation features to turn it into a rap album cover.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"Select an album cover you like\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32969/image/album-cover-maker_2.jpg\"><figcaption>Select an album cover you like</figcaption></figure><h3><b>Step 3</b></h3><p>Click the album cover template you like and it will open in the Placeit album cover maker app.</p><p>Start to customise your album by selecting the background image first. This will set the tone for all your other design choices. </p><p>Go to the lower right hand of the rap album cover maker app and choose an image for the background of your album cover art.</p><p>Note, that if you want to upload your own photo this is where you can do so by clicking on ‘custom image’. Alternatively, you can elect not to use a photo by selecting ‘no image’ and choosing a beautiful colour for your background instead. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"Begin customisation by selecting a background photo\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32969/image/album-cover-maker3.jpg\"><figcaption>Begin customisation by selecting a background photo</figcaption></figure><p>Move to the area above the background photo. This is where you can select an icon to use in your design. This can be the record label’s logo or a symbol associated with the artist. I’ve replaced the shoe with music waves as the record label’s logo. </p><p>You can choose a colour for the logo as well as add colour effects to the photo with the controls above the icon, but I like to leave colour work until later in the process.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"Select a symbol\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32969/image/album-cover-maker_3b.jpg\"><figcaption>Select an icon</figcaption></figure><h3><b>Step 4</b></h3><p>Now we move to the left side of our music album cover maker. </p><p>Starting at the top of the template, you can enter all the relevant text for your rap album cover design—name of album, name of artist, producer, etc.</p><p>Once you’ve entered your text, you can keep the default fonts or select different fonts from the dropdown menu. Again, we will select the colour of the fonts later when we select the colour scheme for the entire album cover design. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"Enter your album details\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32969/image/album-cover-maker_4.jpg\"><figcaption>Enter your album text details and select fonts</figcaption></figure><h3><b>Step 5</b></h3><p>Our next step is to adjust the various elements in the album cover creator so that they fit perfectly together. You can click on each element of the design and move it around the design or click on the corners of an element to scale it up or down. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"Resize elements and move them as needed \" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32969/image/album-cover-maker_5.jpg\"><figcaption>Resize elements and move them as needed </figcaption></figure><p>You should feel free to experiment as much as you like, knowing that if you’ve scaled and/or moved the elements in your album cover design and you aren’t happy with your work, you can simply hit the <strong>Reset Layout</strong> button in top right of the album cover maker app and everything will be reset to its original position. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"Hit the Reset Layout button if you dont like your new layout\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32969/image/album-cover-maker_5a.jpg\"><figcaption>Hit the 'Reset Layout' button if you don't like your new layout</figcaption></figure><h3><b>Step 6</b></h3><p>Now it’s time to customise the colours in your album cover art. You will remember that each element we worked on—fonts, icon, and photo—all have their own colour adjustments that we didn’t touch. </p><p>Well now go back to each one of them and experiment with the colour options provided to find a combination that works for you. If you’ve used a company logo, you should make sure the colour the logo is consistent with the brand. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"Customise the colours of your rap album cover art\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32969/image/album-cover-maker_6.jpg\"><figcaption>Customise the colours of your rap album cover art</figcaption></figure><h3>Step 7<br>\n</h3><p>Look at your rap album cover design as a whole and make any tweaks to the text, fonts, colours, icon or anything else you feel is necessary to make it just right. </p><p>Once you’re satisfied with your design, hit the <strong>Download</strong> button at the top of the screen and download your design for a small fee. Alternatively, if you regularly need to create cool album covers, posters, social media banners, etc., then the monthly plan may be the best deal for you. And that’s it. You’ve got your own customised rap album cover design ready to go. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"Download your design\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32969/image/album-cover-maker_7.jpg\"><figcaption>Download your design</figcaption></figure><h3>Step 8</h3><p>If you want to see what your album cover art would look like in a real-life scenario, upload it to an <a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/mockups/?search=album%20cover\">album cover mockup</a> on Placeit.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/mockups/?search=album%20cover\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Test your rap album cover with a Placeit flyer mockup\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32969/image/rap-album-covers_1.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Test your rap album cover with a <a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/mockups/?search=album%20cover\" target=\"_self\">Placeit album cover mockup</a></figcaption></figure><p>Now that you know how to use the rap album cover maker to make rap album covers, let's take a look at some of the cool album covers you can customise at Placeit.<br></p><h2>\n<b>10 Best Rap A</b>lbum Cover Design </h2><h3>1. <a class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/hip-hop-hits-collection-album-cover-design-maker-465d\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\" Hip-Hop Hits Collection Album Cover cover which obscures the face of the artist and creates a mood of mystery and menace. Make sure your text and icons pop against the dark colours of the cover by using bright text. <br></p><h3>4. <a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/hip-hop-money-album-cover-design-template-465b?multiFolder_Background=d9feb58ffedd8c88af8d499f040bf69e\" target=\"_self\">Hip-Hop Money Album Cover Design Template</a>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/hip-hop-money-album-cover-design-template-465b?multiFolder_Background=d9feb58ffedd8c88af8d499f040bf69e\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Hip-Hop Money Album Cover Design Template\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32969/image/Hip-Hop%20Money%20Album%20Cover%20Design%20Template%20copy.jpg\"></a></figure><p>If you don't have the time or money to do a photo shoot, no worries—the rap album cover maker offers a number of super images that you can use on your cover, like this one that features a break dancer balanced on one hand. Choose the image that most appeals to you, add your text, and your cover is ready to go.<br></p><h3>5. <a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/album-cover-creator-for-blues-cd-472b?multiFolder_Background=b70ac3c7ac36b1e5af6e0a9ccf655b43&amp;textText_T3=-%20Eyes%20On%20Me%20-&amp;textText_T4=ON%20THE%20STREETS%20PRODUCTION&amp;textText_T1=LITTLE%20PRINCE&amp;pos-size_T3=0.3519_0.1926_0.2963_0.0436_d&amp;pos-size_T4=0.3000_0.9350_0.3987_0.0237_d&amp;pos-size_T1=0.2338_0.1113_0.5313_0.0449_d\" target=\"_self\">Album Cover Creator for Blues CD</a>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/hip-hop-money-album-cover-design-template-465b?multiFolder_Background=d9feb58ffedd8c88af8d499f040bf69e\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Album Cover Creator for Blues CD\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32969/image/Album%20Cover%20Creator%20for%20Blues%20CD%20copy.jpg\"></a></figure><p>Try this rap album cover that has been modified using the<a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/album-cover-creator-for-blues-cd-472b?multiFolder_Background=b70ac3c7ac36b1e5af6e0a9ccf655b43&amp;textText_T3=-%20Eyes%20On%20Me%20-&amp;textText_T4=ON%20THE%20STREETS%20PRODUCTION&amp;textText_T1=LITTLE%20PRINCE&amp;pos-size_T3=0.3519_0.1926_0.2963_0.0436_d&amp;pos-size_T4=0.3000_0.9350_0.3987_0.0237_d&amp;pos-size_T1=0.2338_0.1113_0.5313_0.0449_d\" target=\"_self\"> Album Cover Creator for Blues CD</a> template. It features two bars that sandwich the image and is a good choice if you have a particularly strong image you want to focus the viewer's eye on. Use any of the images offered or upload your own and then modify the text as needed. <br></p><h3>6. <a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/alternative-album-cover-maker-with-fluorescent-colors-a49b?multiFolder_Background=476f3451f9b155d5dd435ba8e1b7115b&amp;textText_T1=COME%20HERE\" target=\"_self\">Alternative Album Cover Maker with Fluorescent Colors</a>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/alternative-album-cover-maker-with-fluorescent-colors-a49b?multiFolder_Background=476f3451f9b155d5dd435ba8e1b7115b&amp;textText_T1=COME%20HERE\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Alternative Album Cover Maker with Fluorescent Colors\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32969/image/Screenshot%202019-11-09%20at%209.29.13%20am%20copy.jpg\"></a></figure><p><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/alternative-album-cover-maker-with-fluorescent-colors-a49b?multiFolder_Background=476f3451f9b155d5dd435ba8e1b7115b&amp;textText_T1=COME%20HERE\" target=\"_self\">Alternative Album Cover Maker with Fluorescent Colors</a> is a great template to customise for a rap album cover. It offers tons of terrific photos and a range of fonts that you can experiment with to find the ones that work best for your cover. <br></p><h3>\n<a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/hip-hop-hustle-album-cover-design-maker-465e?textText_T1=Flying%20High&amp;fontText_T1=RubikMonoOne-Regular&amp;multiFolder_Background=9c9f8c036ff8870bef3e76884a9ac954\" target=\"_self\">7. Hip-Hop Hustle Album Cover Design Maker</a><br>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/hip-hop-hustle-album-cover-design-maker-465e?textText_T1=Flying%20High&amp;fontText_T1=RubikMonoOne-Regular&amp;multiFolder_Background=9c9f8c036ff8870bef3e76884a9ac954\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Hip-Hop Hustle Album Cover Design Maker\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32969/image/Hip-Hop%20Hustle%20Album%20Cover%20Design%20Maker%20copy.jpg\"></a></figure><p>The <a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/hip-hop-hustle-album-cover-design-maker-465e?textText_T1=Flying%20High&amp;fontText_T1=RubikMonoOne-Regular&amp;multiFolder_Background=9c9f8c036ff8870bef3e76884a9ac954\" target=\"_self\">Hip-Hop Hustle Album Cover Design Maker</a> template with its party vibe is a great choice for your rap album cover. Just change the text and choose the font and colours you like, and your cover is ready to go. <br></p><h3>8. <a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/jazz-album-cover-maker-with-vintage-images-58e?multiFolder_Main%20Graphic=7e01569cf03faf9f855be44f93aa851d&amp;multiFolder_Logo=q0opiz160a&amp;colorFolder_Logo=#cfe2f3&amp;checkboxText_T1=false&amp;pos-size_Logo=0.0388_0.8865_0.1362_0.0883_d&amp;pos-size_T2=0.5952_0.0506_0.3470_0.0913_d&amp;pos-size_T3=0.5294_0.1603_0.4175_0.0707_d\" target=\"_self\">Jazz Album Cover Maker with Vintage Images</a>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/jazz-album-cover-maker-with-vintage-images-58e?multiFolder_Main%20Graphic=7e01569cf03faf9f855be44f93aa851d&amp;multiFolder_Logo=q0opiz160a&amp;colorFolder_Logo=#cfe2f3&amp;checkboxText_T1=false&amp;pos-size_Logo=0.0388_0.8865_0.1362_0.0883_d&amp;pos-size_T2=0.5952_0.0506_0.3470_0.0913_d&amp;pos-size_T3=0.5294_0.1603_0.4175_0.0707_d\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Jazz Album Cover Maker with Vintage Images\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32969/image/Jazz%20Album%20Cover%20Maker%20with%20Vintage%20Images%20copy.jpg\"></a></figure><p>Use this very special vintage<a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/jazz-album-cover-maker-with-vintage-images-58e?multiFolder_Main%20Graphic=7e01569cf03faf9f855be44f93aa851d&amp;multiFolder_Logo=q0opiz160a&amp;colorFolder_Logo=#cfe2f3&amp;checkboxText_T1=false&amp;pos-size_Logo=0.0388_0.8865_0.1362_0.0883_d&amp;pos-size_T2=0.5952_0.0506_0.3470_0.0913_d&amp;pos-size_T3=0.5294_0.1603_0.4175_0.0707_d\" target=\"_self\"> Jazz Album Cover Maker with Vintage Images</a> template to create a rap album cover with a Motown vibe. Customisation is quick and easy. Add your text and change the overlay colour from rose to whatever colour you prefer. You can upload the parental advisory warning if you need it or add your own logo instead. <br></p><h3>9. <a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/design-template-for-hip-hop-album-465\" target=\"_self\">Hip-Hop Album Design Template</a>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/design-template-for-hip-hop-album-465\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Hip-Hop Album Design Template\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32969/image/Screenshot%202019-11-08%20at%2010.16.30%20pm%20copy.jpg\"></a></figure><p><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/design-template-for-hip-hop-album-465\" target=\"_self\">Hip-Hop Album Design Template</a> is designed specifically for rap album covers. It offers a simple, clean look with tons of gorgeous images and fonts to choose from. As with all the other albums here, it is super easy to customise. <br></p><h3>10. <a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/cool-alternative-music-album-cover-maker-with-dim-colors-a49a?multiFolder_Icon=q0opxva228&amp;checkboxText_T3=false&amp;fontText_T1=ArchivoBlack-Regular&amp;textText_T1=THE%20LOST%20SON&amp;checkboxText_T2=false&amp;pos-size_Icon=0.4250_0.8653_0.1475_0.0945_d&amp;pos-size_T1=0.2338_0.1013_0.4974_0.0461_d\" target=\"_self\">Cool Alternative Music Album Cover Maker with Dim Colors</a>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/cool-alternative-music-album-cover-maker-with-dim-colors-a49a?multiFolder_Icon=q0opxva228&amp;checkboxText_T3=false&amp;fontText_T1=ArchivoBlack-Regular&amp;textText_T1=THE%20LOST%20SON&amp;checkboxText_T2=false&amp;pos-size_Icon=0.4250_0.8653_0.1475_0.0945_d&amp;pos-size_T1=0.2338_0.1013_0.4974_0.0461_d\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Cool Alternative Music Album Cover Maker with Dim Colors\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32969/image/Screenshot%202019-11-09%20at%208.35.15%20am%20copy.jpg\"></a></figure><p>When you're looking for an album cover with a distinct look, check out <a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/cool-alternative-music-album-cover-maker-with-dim-colors-a49a?multiFolder_Icon=q0opxva228&amp;checkboxText_T3=false&amp;fontText_T1=ArchivoBlack-Regular&amp;textText_T1=THE%20LOST%20SON&amp;checkboxText_T2=false&amp;pos-size_Icon=0.4250_0.8653_0.1475_0.0945_d&amp;pos-size_T1=0.2338_0.1013_0.4974_0.0461_d\" target=\"_self\">Cool Alternative Music Album Cover Maker with Dim Colors</a>. Though it wasn't created for rap album covers, it offers terrific abstract images for the background of your album, to which you can add the text you want. In this example, I decided to keep things minimal and modern. <br></p><h2><b>Make Your Own Rap Album Cover Art Today</b></h2><p>Now that you know how to make an album cover online, why not use one of Placeit’s wonderful <a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/?f_devices=Album%20Cover%20Maker&amp;h=42\">album cover templates</a> to make your very own album cover art and share it with us in the comments below.
