//cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx25/cdn13@2020_1/2020/08/24/23-59-52-529_3030d429a6501a3a.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32969/image/Screenshot%202019-11-09%20at%208.35.15%20am%20copy.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn34@2020_3/2020/08/24/23-59-47-868_04ef1f9ed72afbcb.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32263/preview_image/socialmediaimage%20maker.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn77@2020_2/2020/08/24/23-59-50-700_b397b2afe064db28.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32252/preview_image/OnlineFlyer.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn14@2020_1/2020/08/24/23-59-42-884_c926071958ffd7b5.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32356/preview_image/HoodieTemplate!.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn16@2020_3/2020/08/24/23-59-49-773_ad8ddc6fec053da0.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32274/preview_image/mac-mockup.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn45@2020_3/2020/08/24/23-59-42-958_bf7ae23d4c18f7b3.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32168/preview_image/Blaze1.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn62@2020_6/2020/08/24/23-59-53-738_bcb1994ca63d9a4f.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32167/preview_image/BusinessFlyer1.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn93@2020_1/2020/08/24/23-59-43-075_8fb5c6f6cf609be7.webp","http://audio.tutsplus.com.feedsportal.com/c/35227/f/668805/s/32969/sc/4/mf.gif":null,"http://da.feedsportal.com/r/186529796139/u/407/f/668805/c/35227/s/32969/a2.img":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx13/cdn19@2020_3/2020/08/24/23-59-50-258_9d2c0bbe4e2655c2.jpg","http://pi.feedsportal.com/r/186529796139/u/407/f/668805/c/35227/s/32969/a2t.img":null},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598313579864},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 07:59:39","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 07:59:39","title":"All About Avenir & Fonts Similar to Avenir","link":"https://design.tutsplus.com/articles/all-about-avenir-and-fonts-similar-to-avenir--cms-35353","description":"<p>Created by legendary type designer Adrian Frutiger and released in 1988, Avenir is one of the most widely used typefaces in corporate branding. Repeatedly voted by designers as one of the most beautifully designed typefaces, the Avenir font family was Frutiger’s masterwork and continues to be popular in logo design and brand identities today.  </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/0/07/AvenirSP.png\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"avenir font\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/AvenirSP.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/AvenirSP.jpg\"></a></figure><p>Read more about Avenir’s origin story and how this humanist sans serif has gone on to become one of the most iconic fonts in type history. Scroll to the bottom of the article to discover 15 fantastic alternatives to the Avenir font, which offer a contemporary twist on this classic typeface. </p><p>Browse hundreds of <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/fonts/sans-serif\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Link: https://elements.envato.com/fonts/sans-serif\">sans serif fonts</a>, fonts similar to Avenir, Avenir book fonts, and alternatives to Avenir font downloads to use in your design and branding projects on <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/fonts/sans-serif\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Envato Elements</a>.</p><ul class=\"roundup-block__contents posts--half-width roundup-block--card\"><li class=\"roundup-block__content posts__post\"><article><header><a class=\"posts__post-preview\" href=\"https://design.tutsplus.com/articles/everything-you-wanted-to-know-about-helvetica--cms-33404\"><img class=\"posts__post-preview-image posts__post-preview-image--regular\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/33404/preview_image/Preview.jpg\"></a><a class=\"roundup-block__content-link posts__post-title\" href=\"https://design.tutsplus.com/articles/everything-you-wanted-to-know-about-helvetica--cms-33404\"><h1 class=\"nolinks\">Everything You Wanted to Know About Helvetica</h1></a></header><div class=\"posts__post-teaser\">A bona fide celebrity of the type world, the divisive Helvetica typeface has been set on world domination since the 1950s. Possibly the most widely used...</div>\n<footer class=\"posts__post-details\"><div class=\"posts__post-teaser-overlay\"></div>\n<div class=\"posts__post-publication-meta\">\n<img sizes=\"76px\" class=\"posts__post-author_photo\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/profiles/18595/profileImage/Headshot-small.jpg\" alt=\"Grace Fussell\"><div class=\"posts__post-details__info\">\n<address class=\"posts__post-author\"><a class=\"posts__post-author-link\" href=\"https://tutsplus.com/authors/grace-fussell\">Grace Fussell</a></address>\n<time class=\"posts__post-publication-date\" datetime=\"2019-07-16 09:00:00 UTC\" title=\"16 Jul 2019\">16 Jul 2019</time>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"posts__post-primary-category topic-design\"><a class=\"posts__post-primary-category-link topic-design\" href=\"https://design.tutsplus.com/categories/fonts\">Fonts</a></div></footer></article></li></ul><h2>What Is Avenir?</h2><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"avenir typeface\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Avenir.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Avenir.jpg\"></figure><p>Avenir is a <strong>sans serif typeface</strong> in the tradition of <strong>geometric</strong> type styles. Although classified as a geometric typeface, Avenir (which means <em>‘future’ </em>in French) has some <strong>humanist</strong> features which bring warmth and openness to the typeface. </p><p>Avenir is one of the <strong>most</strong> <strong>widely used typefaces in corporate branding</strong>, with many well-known corporations, including banks, rail companies, and food brands, using the font prominently in their logos and brand identities.</p><p>The typeface is exceptionally legible and clear to read, making it highly versatile for use in headers and body text. Avenir paved the way for later humanist geometric sans serifs, such as Freight Sans and Calluna Sans. </p><h2>Who Created the Avenir Typeface?</h2><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adrian frutiger\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Adrian.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Adrian.jpg\"><figcaption>Adrian Frutiger pictured in 2002, towards the end of his period working on Avenir Next alongside Linotype’s in-house type designer Akira Kobayashi. <em>Image from <a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Adrian_Frutiger#/media/File:Adrian_Frutiger_2002_by_Henk_Gianotten.jpg\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Wikimedia Commons</a>.</em></figcaption></figure><p>Avenir was created by legendary Swiss type designer <strong>Adrian Frutiger </strong>(1928-2015), who also created Univers and the self-named Frutiger. Frutiger had dabbled in both sculpture and type design from a very young age, and the influence of the strict, formal cursives taught to him in his Swiss schooldays galvanised him to create more modernist and revolutionary alternatives.</p><p>He worked on Avenir alone, without the help of drafting assistants, and said he designed the typeface with \"human nature in mind\". Avenir was released in three weights in 1988, which later expanded into a six-weight family. </p><p>Frutiger often referred to Avenir as his masterpiece, describing it as \"the hardest typeface I have worked on in my life\". He also referred to the process of creating sans serif typefaces as his “main life’s work”, noting that sans serifs were more difficult to design than serifs due to their stark simplicity.</p><h2>Where Is Avenir Used?</h2><p>The Avenir font family is amongst the most widely used in the world, having been chosen as the corporate typeface for countless companies and organisations.</p><p>For French residents, Avenir is a common feature of everyday life, having been used by France’s national railway company <strong>SNCF</strong> <em>(Société nationale des chemins de fer français)</em> as its corporate typeface since 2013. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"sncf poster using avenir\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/SNCF.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/SNCF.jpg\"><figcaption>An SNCF poster using Avenir. <em>Image from <a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Avenir_(typeface)#/media/File:SNCF_Assistance_Exams_Strasbourg_16_juin_2014.jpg\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Wikimedia Commons</a>.</em></figcaption></figure><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"sncf brand identity\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/SNCF2.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/SNCF2.jpg\"></figure><p>Because of the typeface’s innate familiarity for French citizens, Presidential candidate François Hollande chose Avenir for his election campaign materials. Perhaps in part due to his choice of font, Hollande went on to win the election in 2012.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"hollande campaign\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Equipe-de-campagne.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Equipe-de-campagne.jpg\"><figcaption>Avenir used on the marketing materials for the election campaign of former French president François Hollande in 2012. <em>Image from <a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Avenir_(typeface)#/media/File:Meeting_Bercy_Fran%C3%A7ois_Hollande_29_avril_2012_(12).jpg\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Wikimedia Commons</a>.</em></figcaption></figure><p>British retail and wholesale company <strong>The Co-operative Group</strong> uses Avenir in its corporate identity. Software company <strong>Bloomberg</strong> also uses a customised version of Avenir Next (see below) as its corporate typeface. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"co op foundation branding avenir\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Co-op.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Co-op.jpg\"></figure><p>Tech companies are also not immune to Avenir’s clean, legible appeal. <strong>Apple</strong> chose Avenir for use on its Maps app and some Siri screens in iOS 6, as well as providing pre-loaded versions of Avenir and Avenir Next on OS X Mountain Lion and iWork for iCloud. <strong>Snapchat</strong> has also used Avenir as the app’s main font since 2016.</p><h2>What Were the Different Releases of the Avenir Typeface?</h2><h3>Avenir Next</h3><p>Following the success enjoyed by the original release of Avenir, type foundry <strong>Linotype</strong> returned to Frutiger to invite him to work on an expanded reworking of the Avenir font family. Working alongside the foundry’s in-house designer <strong>Akira Kobayashi</strong>, the pair created <strong>Avenir Next</strong>, publishing the first release of the typeface in 2004. The designers continued to expand the Avenir Next family over the following three years.   </p><p>Widely acclaimed on its release, Avenir Next is a subtly edited version of Avenir. The most notable difference is the more generous tracking (letter-spacing) of Avenir Next, which gives it a more contemporary, airy appearance. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"avenir next typeface\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Avenir-Next-tracking.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Avenir-Next-tracking.jpg\"></figure><p>Electronics company <strong>LG</strong> chose Avenir Next for the button lettering of mobile devices, due to its excellent legibility. British TV channel <strong>BBC2</strong> also broke away from the use of Gill Sans, which is used across other BBC channels, in favour of Avenir Next on their logos and promotional materials to achieve a cleaner, more contemporary brand identity. </p><h3>Avenir Next Rounded</h3><p>Akira Kobayashi returned to Avenir Next with the aim of creating a third generation of Avenir to mark the 25th birthday of Avenir in 2013. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"avenir next rounded font\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Rounded.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Rounded.jpg\"></figure><p>Kobayashi incorporated rounded terminals into the geometric forms of the original Avenir Next typeface, giving the resulting font a ‘sweet-and-salty’ dual personality. Kobayashi pushed the boundaries of Frutiger’s humanist approach to typeface design—<strong>Avenir Next Rounded</strong> has a distinctly mid-century mood and a bouncy, optimistic personality that sets it apart from other geometric sans serifs in the Avenir tradition.</p><h2>The Enduring Appeal of the Avenir Font Family</h2><p>Interestingly, on Fonts.com, Avenir Next is ranked as the #12 best-selling font family, while the original Avenir ranks higher at #5. </p><p>While both Avenir Next and Avenir Next Rounded have been met with acclaim and are widely used in corporate branding, designers still look to the original first-generation Avenir as Frutiger’s masterpiece. Arguably as contemporary and versatile in style and use as when it was first released in the late 1980s, Avenir is credited with being a typeface that is the building block of enduring corporate identities. </p><p><strong>In other words, if you’re creating a brand for a big business, Avenir is a reliable and effective typeface choice, and is likely to look as relevant and contemporary for many years to come. </strong></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"bbc 2 logo branding avenir\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/BBC-Two-logo.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/BBC-Two-logo.jpg\"><figcaption>Avenir Next in use on the corporate identity for British television channel BBC Two.</figcaption></figure><p>Perhaps you’ve used Avenir in a design project and are interested in discovering similar alternatives. You’re not short of options—a wide range of designers have used Avenir as a principal point of inspiration for their own typeface designs, looking to the humanist design tradition established by Frutiger to inform cutting-edge sans serifs which perhaps offer something a little different to the Avenir font family. </p><p>From mid-century infused <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/bw-modelica-font-family-96W3JH\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Link: https://elements.envato.com/bw-modelica-font-family-96W3JH\">Bw Modelica</a> to faithful Avenir tribute <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/liber-v2-QXUX97\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Liber</a>, contemporary type designers always come back to Avenir as a source of creative inspiration.</p><p>Discover your next favourite font, from Avenir book fonts to branding fonts, from the list of Avenir tributes below. </p><h2>15 Fonts Similar to Avenir</h2><p>Looking for a cheaper <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/fonts/sans-serif\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Link: https://elements.envato.com/fonts/sans-serif\">alternative to Avenir</a>, or a contemporary twist on the classic typeface? These 15 fonts take their cues from Avenir’s sleek, minimalist styling, with modern-day tweaks to bring the much-loved style bang up-to-date for print and web design. </p><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">1.</span> <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/liber-v2-QXUX97\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Liber</a>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/liber-v2-QXUX97\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"liber font\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Liber.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Liber.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/liber-v2-QXUX97\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Liber sans serif font family</a></figcaption></figure><p>Designed by Valerio Dell’Edera in 2016, <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/liber-v2-QXUX97\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Liber</a> pays tribute to the heritage of Avenir and Futura but refines the style for the 21st century. Built on ‘the mathematical purity of geometric circles and clarity of squares’, Liber is ultra-legible, with a harmonious, calming appearance.</p><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">2.</span> <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/bw-modelica-font-family-96W3JH\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Link: https://elements.envato.com/bw-modelica-font-family-96W3JH\">Bw Modelica</a>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/bw-modelica-font-family-96W3JH\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"modelica\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Modelica.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Modelica.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/bw-modelica-font-family-96W3JH\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Bw Modelica geometric sans serif font.</a></figcaption></figure><p>Created by Alberto Romanos, <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/bw-modelica-font-family-96W3JH\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Bw Modelica</a> is a minimal and reliable geometric sans serif with an open, friendly appearance. With its clean style and generous x-height, this exceptionally broad font family (containing 64 styles) is adaptable for both body and headline copy.</p><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">3.</span> <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/berlin-minimal-sans-serif-typeface-web-font-S98HND\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">BERLIN</a>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/berlin-minimal-sans-serif-typeface-web-font-S98HND\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"berlin font\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Berline.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Berline.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/berlin-minimal-sans-serif-typeface-web-font-S98HND\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Berlin sans serif display font.</a></figcaption></figure><p>Designed by SIGNIA PRO designers Fontastica, <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/berlin-minimal-sans-serif-typeface-web-font-S98HND\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">BERLIN</a> is ultra-minimal, clean, and contemporary, exaggerating the geometric heritage of Avenir and its counterparts. Use it in headlines, across minimal packaging designs, and in fashion and lifestyle branding to make the most of its cutting-edge good looks.</p><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">4.</span> <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/frank-F37JU9\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Frank</a>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/frank-F37JU9\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"frank font\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Frank.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Frank.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/frank-F37JU9\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Frank display font family.</a></figcaption></figure><p>Inspired by Futura and stricter geometric sans serifs, <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/frank-F37JU9\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Frank</a> is available in five weights and more than 300 glyphs. The Avenir-style typeface is designed with display and web design in mind.</p><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">5.</span> <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/lorin-modern-geometric-typeface-web-fonts-X7668N\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Lorin</a>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/lorin-modern-geometric-typeface-web-fonts-X7668N\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"lorin font\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Lorin.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Lorin.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/lorin-modern-geometric-typeface-web-fonts-X7668N\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Lorin geometric sans serif font.</a></figcaption></figure><p>Released by foundry Fontastica, creators of BERLIN (above), <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/lorin-modern-geometric-typeface-web-fonts-X7668N\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Lorin</a> is a quietly designed rounded sans serif that lifts inspiration from Frutiger’s type designs. Stylish and feminine, Lorin is a great fit for branding and poster projects. </p><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">6.</span> <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/hamlin-minimal-geometric-typeface-web-fonts-6H38WJ\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Hamlin</a> </h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/hamlin-minimal-geometric-typeface-web-fonts-6H38WJ\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"hamlin\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Hamlin.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Hamlin.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/hamlin-minimal-geometric-typeface-web-fonts-6H38WJ\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Hamlin minimal font family.</a></figcaption></figure><p>An ultra-minimalist sans serif also designed by Fontastica, <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/hamlin-minimal-geometric-typeface-web-fonts-6H38WJ\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Hamlin</a> lifts influences from Frutiger’s humanist designs for Avenir but adds more contemporary character. Use it across packaging and website layouts for a minimal, clean, and exceptionally stylish look and feel.</p><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">7.</span> <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/brooklyn-minimal-geometric-sans-serif-typeface-BSA7LPQ\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">BROOKLYN</a>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/brooklyn-minimal-geometric-sans-serif-typeface-BSA7LPQ\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"brooklyn\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Brrooklyn.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Brrooklyn.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/brooklyn-minimal-geometric-sans-serif-typeface-BSA7LPQ\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Brooklyn geometric typeface family.</a></figcaption></figure><p>A cosier take on the geometric sans serif style, Brooklyn’s reduced x-height gives it a sturdy, 90s-inspired appearance. Beautiful across logos and packaging, this is a font built for branding projects.</p><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">8.</span> <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/herz-simple-sans-serif-typeface-7CCL3A\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Herz</a>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/herz-simple-sans-serif-typeface-7CCL3A\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"herz\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Herz.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Herz.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/herz-simple-sans-serif-typeface-7CCL3A\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Herz everyday typeface.</a></figcaption></figure><p>Available in three weights and as both a desktop and web font, <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/herz-simple-sans-serif-typeface-7CCL3A\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Link: https://elements.envato.com/herz-simple-sans-serif-typeface-7CCL3A\">Herz</a> has a retro, condensed style that is reminiscent of Akzidenz Grotesk and Futura. Simple, friendly, and versatile, Herz is legible both at large display size and for smaller body copy.</p><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">9.</span> <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/noir-pro-928A3Z\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Noir Pro</a>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/noir-pro-928A3Z\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"noir pro\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Noir%20Pro.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Noir Pro.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/noir-pro-928A3Z\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Noir Pro typeface family.</a></figcaption></figure><p>Inspired by the early 20th century sans serifs which also influenced Frutiger’s type designs, <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/noir-pro-928A3Z\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Noir Pro</a> is elegant and organic, with a broad range of weights ranging from light to heavy. A beautiful typeface for using on poster designs and other print work. </p><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">10.</span> <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/regime-grotesk-R87LSR\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Regime Grotesk</a>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/regime-grotesk-R87LSR\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"regime grotesk\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Regime%20Grotesk.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Regime Grotesk.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/regime-grotesk-R87LSR\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Regime Grotesk font family.</a></figcaption></figure><p>Quoting its inspiration as stemming from 1920s Italian design, <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/regime-grotesk-R87LSR\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Regime Grotesk</a> pays tribute to the quirks of typefaces from this era, such as Futura and Mostra. The font is designed to be balanced, modern, and easily adaptable for web, print, or signage design.</p><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">11.</span> <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/normal-minimal-sans-serif-typeface-webfonts-YH9DF3\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Normal</a>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/normal-minimal-sans-serif-typeface-webfonts-YH9DF3\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"normal font\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Normal.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Normal.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/normal-minimal-sans-serif-typeface-webfonts-YH9DF3\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Normal minimal font family.</a></figcaption></figure><p>Pure and minimal, <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/normal-minimal-sans-serif-typeface-webfonts-YH9DF3\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Normal</a> is an everyday font with added style. Tailored for logotypes, headlines, branding materials, and corporate identities, Normal looks fantastic paired with colourful, modernist-inspired graphics and black-and-white photography.</p><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">12.</span> <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/konnect-font-family-DQ384M\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Konnect</a>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/konnect-font-family-DQ384M\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"konnect font\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Konnect.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Konnect.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/konnect-font-family-DQ384M\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Konnect quirky geometric font.</a></figcaption></figure><p>Lifting influences from classical and contemporary type styles, and blending these with more playful elements, <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/konnect-font-family-DQ384M\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Link: https://elements.envato.com/konnect-font-family-DQ384M\">Konnect</a> is a sans serif with soul. The curving ligatures give the typeface a dynamic quality that is reminiscent of mid-century and 1960s sans serifs. </p><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">13.</span> <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/ca-saygon-text-BKV3GCQ\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">CA Saygon Text</a>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/ca-saygon-text-BKV3GCQ\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"saygon text\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Saygon%20text.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Saygon text.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/ca-saygon-text-BKV3GCQ\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Saygon Text typeface family.</a></figcaption></figure><p>The sister of <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/ca-saygon-TU78A5N\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">CA Saygon</a>, <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/ca-saygon-text-BKV3GCQ\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">CA Saygon Text</a> was created by the Cape Arcona foundry to provide a calmer alternative to the original typeface. Inspired by early static grotesque typefaces such as Akzidenz Grotesk, which also inspired Frutiger’s designs for Avenir, CA Saygon Text has a large range of stylistic sets with letter variation, making for a fun, versatile font family for designers to use.</p><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">14.</span> <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/bergen-text-LDBYM2\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Bergen Text</a>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/bergen-text-LDBYM2\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"bergen text\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Bergen%20Text.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Bergen Text.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/bergen-text-LDBYM2\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Bergen Text sans serif typeface.</a></figcaption></figure><p>Released by Mindburger Studio, <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/bergen-text-LDBYM2\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Bergen Text</a> is the companion font to Bergen Sans. Designed to be highly legible while retaining personality, this is a bouncier alternative to more traditional geometric sans serifs like Avenir.</p><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">15.</span> <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/bergen-mono-942DQ4\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Link: https://elements.envato.com/bergen-mono-942DQ4\">Bergen Mono</a>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/bergen-mono-942DQ4\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"bergen mono\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Bergen%20Mono.jpg\" title=\"Image: https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/35353/image/Bergen Mono.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/bergen-mono-942DQ4\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Bergen Mono typeface.</a></figcaption></figure><p>A monospaced take on sans serif type styles and also released by Mindburger Studio, <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/bergen-mono-942DQ4\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Bergen Mono</a> balances retro functionality with a clean, contemporary style. Use it on magazine design, posters, and signage to make the most of its vintage good looks.</p><p>Learn about other classic fonts and alternatives for celebrated typefaces, such as Helvetica:</p><ul class=\"roundup-block__contents posts--half-width roundup-block--card\">\n<li class=\"roundup-block__content posts__post\"><article><header><a class=\"posts__post-preview\" href=\"https://design.tutsplus.com/articles/everything-you-wanted-to-know-about-helvetica--cms-33404\"><img class=\"posts__post-preview-image posts__post-preview-image--regular\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/33404/preview_image/Preview.jpg\"></a><a class=\"roundup-block__content-link posts__post-title\" href=\"https://design.tutsplus.com/articles/everything-you-wanted-to-know-about-helvetica--cms-33404\"><h1 class=\"nolinks\">Everything You Wanted to Know About Helvetica</h1></a></header><div class=\"posts__post-teaser\">A bona fide celebrity of the type world, the divisive Helvetica typeface has been set on world domination since the 1950s. Possibly the most widely used...</div>\n<footer class=\"posts__post-details\"><div class=\"posts__post-teaser-overlay\"></div>\n<div class=\"posts__post-publication-meta\">\n<img sizes=\"76px\" class=\"posts__post-author_photo\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/profiles/18595/profileImage/Headshot-small.jpg\" alt=\"Grace Fussell\"><div class=\"posts__post-details__info\">\n<address class=\"posts__post-author\"><a class=\"posts__post-author-link\" href=\"https://tutsplus.com/authors/grace-fussell\">Grace Fussell</a></address>\n<time class=\"posts__post-publication-date\" datetime=\"2019-07-16 09:00:00 UTC\" title=\"16 Jul 2019\">16 Jul 2019</time>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"posts__post-primary-category topic-design\"><a class=\"posts__post-primary-category-link topic-design\" href=\"https://design.tutsplus.com/categories/fonts\">Fonts</a></div></footer></article></li>\n<li class=\"roundup-block__content posts__post\"><article><header><a class=\"posts__post-preview\" href=\"https://design.tutsplus.com/articles/15-fonts-similar-to-helvetica--cms-33388\"><img class=\"posts__post-preview-image posts__post-preview-image--regular\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/33388/preview_image/Preview.jpg\"></a><a class=\"roundup-block__content-link posts__post-title\" href=\"https://design.tutsplus.com/articles/15-fonts-similar-to-helvetica--cms-33388\"><h1 class=\"nolinks\">15 Fonts Similar to Helvetica</h1></a></header><div class=\"posts__post-teaser\">Looking for fonts similar to Helvetica? href=\"https://design.tutsplus.com/articles/the-rise-of-the-sans-serif--cms-33548\"><h1 class=\"nolinks\">The Rise of the Sans Serif</h1></a></header><div class=\"posts__post-teaser\">In this article, You'll learn what makes them great and discover some options for your next project.</div>\n<footer class=\"posts__post-details\"><div class=\"posts__post-teaser-overlay\"></div>\n<div With minimal graphics, this one especially benefits from custom fonts and text overlays to bring your team name to the forefront.</p><h3>19. <a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/logos/stages/sci-fi-game-channel-logo-maker-1457b\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Sci-fi Game Channel Logo Maker</a>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/logos/stages/sci-fi-game-channel-logo-maker-1457b\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Sci-Fi Game Channel Logo Maker\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/151/posts/32740/image/19.jpg\"></a></figure><p>Sci-fi has been a popular genre for decades, and this video game logo maker is the perfect way to capture it. It brings with it a unique style that’s difficult to replicate. But this logo for gaming teams does the difficult job perfectly. For a retro yet timeless branding style, no template does better.</p><h3>20. <a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/logos/stages/gaming-logo-creator-with-hipster-avatar-1460b\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Gaming Logo Creator with Hipster Avatar</a>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/logos/stages/gaming-logo-creator-with-hipster-avatar-1460b\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Gaming Logo Creator with Hipster Avatar\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/151/posts/32740/image/20.jpg\"></a></figure><p>Hipster design elements are an easy way to show off your gaming team’s modern style. And thanks to this custom Placeit template, they’ve never been easier to roll into your branding. Select custom accessories and primary logo designs to customize your brand style. And don’t forget to experiment with the variety of color placeholders to make things truly your own.</p><h3>How to Make Your Own Video Game Logo Quickly</h3><p><a href=\"https://placeit.net/gaming-logo-maker\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Placeit</a> is the best option for quick and easy graphic design today. It features thousands of professional, custom design templates for video game logos. All you've got to do is choose one you like and then drop in your own content. </p><p>Once your design is complete, simply click \"Download\", and your finished video game logo will be ready to use. Truly, all you've got to do is fill in the blanks and then enjoy the amazing results.</p><h3><b>1. 07:59:39","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 07:59:39","title":"15 Fonts Similar to Gotham","link":"https://design.tutsplus.com/articles/15-fonts-similar-to-gotham--cms-35407","description":"<p>Looking for fonts similar to Gotham? In this article, you'll find some of the best Gotham font alternatives to use on your next projects.<br></p><p>Gotham is one of the latest fonts to take over the world. While it was developed quite recently, the font has already been part of world-changing causes. Gotham font designer Tobias Frere-Jones was inspired by mid-20th century architectural signage. The result is a neutral, geometric, and straightforward sans serif. Gotham was used on the Freedom Tower (the main building of the rebuilt World Trade Center), the Obama campaign, and commercial brands like Saturday Night Live, Tom Ford, and Chanel. </p><p>In this article, we'll provide you with 15 Gotham font alternatives. This is perfect if you want to find something similar and affordable. Looking for more high-quality <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/fonts/sans-serif/sans+serif/spacing-normal/sort-by-latest\" target=\"_self\">sans serif fonts</a>? Be sure to check out <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/\" target=\"_self\">Envato Elements</a> and <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/\" target=\"_self\">GraphicRiver</a> to explore their extensive library. </p><h2><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/signia-pro-modern-typeface-webfont-JVJLJW\" target=\"_self\">Signia</a></h2><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/signia-pro-modern-typeface-webfont-JVJLJW\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Gotham font alternative Signia\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2056/posts/35407/image/FontsLikeGotham-Signia.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/signia-pro-modern-typeface-webfont-JVJLJW\" target=\"_self\">Signia</a></figcaption></figure><p>Signia is a great Gotham font alternative. This ultra-modern sans serif is inspired by street lettering styles. The characters have a wide aperture, which is a signature of the Gotham font family. This pack comes with two font weights, and if you're looking for a similar Gotham web font, this one also includes a web version! </p><h2><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/signal-modern-display-headline-typeface-4F4F3N\" target=\"_self\">Signal</a></h2><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/signal-modern-display-headline-typeface-4F4F3N\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Gotham font alternative Signal\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2056/posts/35407/image/FontsLikeGotham-Signal.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/signal-modern-display-headline-typeface-4F4F3N\" target=\"_self\">Signal</a></figcaption></figure><p>We all can recognize the characteristic G on Gotham. Signal is one of the few fonts similar to Gotham that includes the key character. Use this font for display text, branding, and headlines. It includes five weights from light to heavy, so you're sure to catch someone's attention. </p><h2><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/nord-minimal-display-headline-logo-typeface-48EKN7H\" target=\"_self\">Nord</a></h2><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/nord-minimal-display-headline-logo-typeface-48EKN7H\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Gotham font alternative Nord\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2056/posts/35407/image/FontsLikeGotham-Nord.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/nord-minimal-display-headline-logo-typeface-48EKN7H\" target=\"_self\">Nord</a></figcaption></figure><p>This minimal and modern sans serif has to be the closest font to Gotham. Nord is a modern sans serif that has similar proportions to the original Gotham typeface. With many capabilities, the typeface comes with seven weights, from thin to black, each with its own italic version. </p><h2><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/oliviar-sans-regular-family-PTNTR3A\" target=\"_self\">Oliviar Sans</a></h2><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/oliviar-sans-regular-family-PTNTR3A\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Gotham font alternative Oliviar Sans\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2056/posts/35407/image/FontsLikeGotham-OliviaSansRegular.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/oliviar-sans-regular-family-PTNTR3A\" target=\"_self\">Oliviar Sans</a></figcaption></figure><p>The Gotham Ultra font is a visually strong family that won't go unnoticed if used on a project. Oliviar Sans is an awesome dupe for fonts like Gotham. This modern sans is inspired by geometrical sans serif fonts. The pack includes seven weights and multiple language support. So if you're looking for a Gotham black font or a Gotham bold font, this pack includes those options and more. </p><h2><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/hamlin-minimal-geometric-typeface-web-fonts-6H38WJ\" target=\"_self\">Hamlin</a></h2><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/hamlin-minimal-geometric-typeface-web-fonts-6H38WJ\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Gotham font alternative Hamlin\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2056/posts/35407/image/FontsLikeGotham-Hamlin.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/hamlin-minimal-geometric-typeface-web-fonts-6H38WJ\" target=\"_self\">Hamlin</a></figcaption></figure><p>Hamlin is inspired by classic geometric fonts similar to Gotham. This modern sans serif is a contemporary take on the minimalist design trend. The font is suitable for body copy, a perfect replacement for the Gotham book font version. Use it on brand identities, headlines, and many more projects. </p><h2><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/normal-minimal-sans-serif-typeface-webfonts-YH9DF3\" target=\"_self\">Normal</a></h2><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/normal-minimal-sans-serif-typeface-webfonts-YH9DF3\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Gotham font alternative Normal\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2056/posts/35407/image/FontsLikeGotham-Norma.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/normal-minimal-sans-serif-typeface-webfonts-YH9DF3\" target=\"_self\">Normal</a></figcaption></figure><p>This unique font is minimal but with a twist. The wide apertures in the lowercase characters are an attribute of fonts like Gotham. Normal includes five weights, ranging from extra light to extra bold. If you're looking for a Gotham light font or a Gotham medium font lookalike, Normal is a great choice.<br></p><h2><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/berlin-minimal-sans-serif-typeface-web-font-S98HND\" target=\"_self\">Berlin</a></h2><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/berlin-minimal-sans-serif-typeface-web-font-S98HND\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Gotham font alternative Berlin\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2056/posts/35407/image/FontsLikeGotham-Berlin.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/berlin-minimal-sans-serif-typeface-web-font-S98HND\" target=\"_self\">Berlin</a></figcaption></figure><p>Great options for Gotham web fonts are hard to come by. Berlin was designed with perfection in mind. The attention to detail in each character makes it suitable for both display and body copy. Use the bold version as an alternative to a Gotham bold font for a polished and minimalist look. </p><h2><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/visia-pro-elegant-geometric-typeface-web-fonts-V6N6VU\" target=\"_self\">Visia Pro</a></h2><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/visia-pro-elegant-geometric-typeface-web-fonts-V6N6VU\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Gotham font alternative Visia Pro\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2056/posts/35407/image/FontsLikeGotham-VisiaPro.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/visia-pro-elegant-geometric-typeface-web-fonts-V6N6VU\" target=\"_self\">Visia Pro</a></figcaption></figure><p>Typefaces inspired by geometric figures are the closest fonts to Gotham. Visia Pro is the perfect mix of elegant and minimalist font aesthetics. This great Gotham font alternative comes with seven weights, each with its own italic version. Use this versatile font on any type of project, from logos to editorial design. </p><h2><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/berlin-rounded-sans-serif-display-typeface-J4FPDN\" target=\"_self\">Berlin Rounded</a></h2><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/berlin-rounded-sans-serif-display-typeface-J4FPDN\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Gotham font alternative Berlin Rounded\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2056/posts/35407/image/FontsLikeGotham-BerlinRounded.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/berlin-rounded-sans-serif-display-typeface-J4FPDN\" target=\"_self\">Berlin Rounded</a></figcaption></figure><p>The Gotham rounded font is an adaptation of the original Gotham that celebrates precision. Berlin Rounded is a version of Berlin, and rest assured that this font was designed with perfection in mind. Rounded fonts convey easiness and appear friendly compared to their original versions. This pack comes with four weights, and web fonts are included. </p><h2><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/bw-modelica-condensed-font-family-KYBFGJ\" target=\"_self\">Modelica Condensed</a></h2><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/bw-modelica-condensed-font-family-KYBFGJ\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Gotham font alternative Modelica Condensed\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2056/posts/35407/image/FontsLikeGotham-ModelicaCondensed.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/bw-modelica-condensed-font-family-KYBFGJ\" target=\"_self\">Modelica Condensed</a></figcaption></figure><p>Modelica Condensed is a minimalist geometric font, designed with clean shapes and a tall x-height. The original Gotham typeface includes four different widths, and Modelica Condensed is a great alternative for a Gotham narrow font. The generous x-height makes it suitable for body copy. The font is available in four widths, and each one has eight weights, with matching oblique italics. That's 64 styles for you to explore!</p><h2><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/lorano-family-RP4P9V\" target=\"_self\">Lorano</a></h2><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/lorano-family-RP4P9V\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Gotham font alternative Lorano\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2056/posts/35407/image/FontsLikeGotham-Lorano.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/lorano-family-RP4P9V\" target=\"_self\">Lorano</a></figcaption></figure><p>Lorano is a powerful geometric font that's inspired by minimalism. The pack includes 13 weights, so it's just as extensive as the Gotham typeface. This set covers anything from a Gotham light font to Gotham Book and even a Gotham Ultra font. It supports many languages, so you're set if you work in the editorial design world. </p><h2><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/ripple-minimal-modern-sans-serif-typeface-J9AXVKL\" target=\"_self\">Ripple</a></h2><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/ripple-minimal-modern-sans-serif-typeface-J9AXVKL\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Gotham font alternative Ripple\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2056/posts/35407/image/FontsLikeGotham-Ripple.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/ripple-minimal-modern-sans-serif-typeface-J9AXVKL\" target=\"_self\">Ripple</a></figcaption></figure><p>The Gotham font family includes many font weights. Ripple is a modern font with many capabilities. It's ideal for designing logos and corporate identities, and it's suitable for print and web. One of the many capabilities of Ripple is that it includes six font weights. You'll find replacements for anything from a Gotham medium font to a Gotham black font.  </p><h2><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/bolt-rounded-modern-typeface-webfont-7HVBBU\" target=\"_self\">Bolt</a></h2><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/bolt-rounded-modern-typeface-webfont-7HVBBU\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Gotham font alternative Bolt\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2056/posts/35407/image/FontsLikeGotham-BoltRounded.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/bolt-rounded-modern-typeface-webfont-7HVBBU\" target=\"_self\">Bolt</a></figcaption></figure><p>Looking for a Gotham rounded font lookalike? Bolt is a minimal sans serif with rounded corners. This clean font is the perfect choice if you want something classic in your design. In addition to the regular font files, the pack also includes web fonts ready to be used!</p><h2><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/prox-VUT9GZ\" target=\"_self\">Prox</a></h2><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/prox-VUT9GZ\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Gotham font alternative Prox\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2056/posts/35407/image/FontsLikeGotham-Prox.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/prox-VUT9GZ\" target=\"_self\">Prox</a></figcaption></figure><p>Prox is a narrow sans serif very close to the Gotham narrow font. It has a slightly squared proportion on the characters and open apertures, making it extremely legible. The pack comes with two weights, regular and bold, each with an italic version. </p><h2><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/giga-sans-RTMN9EK\" target=\"_self\">Giga Sans</a></h2><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/giga-sans-RTMN9EK\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Gotham font alternative Giga Sans\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2056/posts/35407/image/FontsLikeGotham-GigaSans.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/giga-sans-RTMN9EK\" target=\"_self\">Giga Sans</a></figcaption></figure><p>Giga Sans is a super clean geometric sans serif. To find fonts similar to Gotham Book, you need to look for an extended family with different weights. Giga Sans includes nine weights, and each has an italic version. You can use it anywhere from headlines to body copy and display. </p><h2>Conclusion</h2><p>Gotham font designer Tobias Frere-Jones was inspired by street signs around New York. Since its release in 2000, Gotham has been used in many commercial brands and even Barack Obama's 2008 campaign. The font has already made history, but it also has become ever-present. In this article, we showed you the 15 best Gotham font alternatives to use on your next project. Are there any other font dupes you're looking for? Let us know in the comments section below!</p><p>Looking for more fonts similar to <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/fonts/sans-serif/gotham+book/spacing-normal\" target=\"_self\">Gotham Book</a>? assets. </p><p>If you like this Gotham typeface article, be sure to check out:</p><ul class=\"roundup-block__contents posts--half-width roundup-block--list\">\n<li class=\"roundup-block__content\"><a /24/23-59-42-709_f213ffe848e08aee.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2056/posts/35407/image/FontsLikeGotham-Lorano.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn48@2020_1/2020/08/24/23-59-45-245_96e16d4df2e143c9.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2056/posts/35407/image/FontsLikeGotham-Ripple.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn32@2020_2/2020/08/24/23-59-49-809_198bd5d5200625db.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2056/posts/35407/image/FontsLikeGotham-BoltRounded.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn42@2020_4/2020/08/24/23-59-44-356_fa94b333fe8171f3.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2056/posts/35407/image/FontsLikeGotham-Prox.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn56@2020_1/2020/08/24/23-59-47-419_05d64cbce2adb8af.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2056/posts/35407/image/FontsLikeGotham-GigaSans.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn27@2020_4/2020/08/24/23-59-51-063_a6e86951df2bace5.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/33388/preview_image/Preview.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn26@2020_2/2020/08/24/23-59-44-257_2f2c1011c4574ce9.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/35057/preview_image/VintageFont.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx2/cdn7@2020_5/2020/08/24/23-59-47-113_d9fd049f7851d85f.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2056/posts/35034/preview_image/3-2-JournalismMagazine-Mondia-thumbnail.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx14/cdn49@2020_3/2020/08/24/23-59-48-061_f407cbb916b2b07a.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/114/posts/33836/preview_image/Preview.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn96@2020_5/2020/08/24/23-59-51-678_382ee7168c50d54d.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2056/posts/33460/preview_image/Basic%20Typography%20article%20-24.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn8@2 07:59:39","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 07:59:39","title":"How to Create a Pastel Color Swatch in Photoshop","link":"https://design.tutsplus.com/tutorials/how-to-create-a-pastel-color-swatch-in-photoshop--cms-35536","description":"<figure class=\"final-product final-product--image\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35536/final_image/pastel%20color%20codes%20tutorial%20main%20preview.jpg\" alt=\"Final product image\"><!--googleoff: index--><figcaption>What You'll Be Creating</figcaption><!--googleon: index--></figure><p>What are pastel colors? They're usually described as colors with high value and low saturation. Solid pastel colors fit perfectly with fashion, web, and any other designs with their pale color combinations. So, in today's pastel color Photoshop tutorial, we are going to explore the default pastel color palette in Photoshop, and then we'll create our own pastel color scheme with the color picker tool and discover some useful pastel color codes. Finally, we will create a pastel palette Photoshop scheme with Adobe Color.</p><p>If you want to learn about Photoshop pastel color palettes via video, check out our lesson on the <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/user/TutsPremium\" target=\"_self\">Envato Tuts+ YouTube channel</a>:</p><figure data-video-embed=\"true\" data-original-url=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=C9PvFw47Avk\" class=\"embedded-video\">\n  <iframe src=\"//www.youtube.com/embed/C9PvFw47Avk?rel=0\" webkitallowfullscreen=\"webkitallowfullscreen\" mozallowfullscreen=\"mozallowfullscreen\" allowfullscreen=\"allowfullscreen\" frameborder=\"0\"></iframe>\n</figure><h2>What You'll Learn in This Pastel Color Photoshop Tutorial</h2><ul>\n<li>How to access the default pastel colors in Photoshop<br>\n</li>\n<li>How to create your own pastel color scheme using the default Color Libraries</li>\n<li>How to create a Photoshop pastel color palette using the Color Picker tool</li>\n<li>How to create a pastel color palette in Photoshop with Adobe Color</li>\n<li>Useful pastel color code Photoshop examples</li>\n</ul><h2>Tutorial Assets</h2><p>The following assets were used during the production of this tutorial:<br></p><ul>\n<li><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/pastel-french-macaroons-L79KUHF\" target=\"_self\" title=\"Link: https://elements.envato.com/ru/pastel-french-macaroons-L79KUHF\">Photo of French Macaroons</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/riga-latvia-famous-landmark-television-tower-in-pi-PSND9VP\" target=\"_self\" title=\"Link: https://elements.envato.com/ru/riga-latvia-famous-landmark-television-tower-in-pi-PSND9VP\">Photo of Riga</a></li>\n</ul><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">1.</span> <b>How to Access the Default Pastel Colors in Photoshop<br></b>\n</h2><h3>Step 1</h3><p>There are two ways to open the default color libraries in Photoshop. Let's start with the <strong>Color Picker</strong> tool, click on the <strong>Foreground Color,</strong> and then select <strong>Color Libraries</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"Opening the color libraries\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35536/image/Opening%20the%20color%20libraries.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 2</h3><p>Press the <strong>Book</strong> button to see all the available libraries.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"Selecting the color library\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35536/image/Selecting%20the%20color%20library.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 3</h3><p>The second way to open the color library is to go to <strong>Window &gt; Swatches </strong>and then hit <strong>Icon</strong> in the top-right corner of the <strong>Swatches</strong> panel. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"opening the swatches panel\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35536/image/opening%20the%20swatches%20panel.jpg\"></figure><p>And here you can see all the available default color libraries.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"opening the color libraries in the swatches panel\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35536/image/opening%20the%20color%20libraries%20in%20the%20swatches%20panel.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 4</h3><p>The main difference between these two methods is that when you open the color library in the Swatches panel, it automatically adds all the colors as swatches. If you open the color library in the <strong>Color Picker</strong>, it shows you the colors in the right column and different variations of the selected color in the left column.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"color libraries in swatches panel and in color picker tool\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35536/image/color%20libraries%20in%20swatches%20panel%20and%20in%20color%20picker%20tool.jpg\"></figure><p>I can recommend the following libraries where you can find pastel colors: <br></p><ul>\n<li>ANPA colors</li>\n<li>Pantone+ Solid Uncoated<br>\n</li>\n<li>Pantone+ Pastel&amp;Neons<br>\n</li>\n</ul><p>Here are some examples of the Photoshop pastel color palette I created with these libraries:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"example of color schemes created with color libraries\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35536/image/example%20of%20color%20schemes%20created%20with%20color%20libraries.jpg\"></figure><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">2.</span> <b>How to Create Your Own Pastel Color Scheme Using the Default Color Libraries</b>\n</h2><h3>Step 1</h3><p>Let's open the ANPA color library with a lot of solid pastel colors. As you can see, the first four colors of this library have a pretty low saturation with high value settings and could be useful for creating your own pastel color schemes.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"selecting the pastel color from color library\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35536/image/selecting%20the%20pastel%20color%20from%20color%20library.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 2</h3><p>To add a new swatch, you should select the variation of the color that you like, and then hit <strong>Picker </strong>and select <strong>Add to Swatches</strong>. Now we have access to the desired color in our <strong>Swatches</strong> panel. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adding a color from the library to the swatches\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35536/image/adding%20a%20color%20from%20the%20library%20to%20the%20swatches.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 3</h3><p>Let's add four more colors using the same method. I chose purple, turquoise, green, and yellow.  As you can see, it's pretty easy to create your own pastel preset Photoshop color schemes using the ANPA color library.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating a pastel color scheme using color library\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35536/image/creating%20a%20pastel%20color%20scheme%20using%20color%20library.jpg\"></figure><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">3.</span> How to Create a Photoshop Pastel Color Palette Using the Color Picker Tool</h2><p>Now let's create a pastel gradient Photoshop color scheme using a color picker and the image of the sunset. Open the <strong>Color Picker</strong> tool, and then select the colors sequentially and add them to swatches.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35536/image/creating%20a%20color%20palette%20from%20an%20image.jpg\"></figure><p>This is how our pastel gradient Photoshop color scheme looks:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"pastel color palette from the image\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35536/image/pastel%20color%20palette%20from%20the%20image.jpg\"></figure><p>And here's another example of pastel preset Photoshop swatches created with colors from another image:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"second example of color palette created with color picker\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35536/image/second%20example%20of%20color%20palette%20created%20with%20color%20picker.jpg\"></figure><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">4.</span> How to Create Pastel Color Palette Photoshop Swatches Using Adobe Color</h2><h3>Step 1</h3><p>In this section of our pastel color Photoshop tutorial, let's try <a href=\"https://color.adobe.com/create/color-wheel\" target=\"_self\">Adobe Color</a> for creating pastel palettes. In the left column, you can see different harmony rules, and before creating your new pastel palette, you need to select the one you want to use.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"selecting the color harmony rule\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35536/image/selecting%20the%20color%20harmony%20rule.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 2</h3><p><span class=\"sectionnum\">I choose the <strong>Square </strong>harmony rule for my P</span>hotoshop pastel color palette. To get pastel color code Photoshop presets, you need to keep the points near the center of the circle. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"selecting the pastel colors in the color wheel\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35536/image/selecting%20the%20pastel%20colors%20in%20the%20color%20wheel.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 3</h3><p><span class=\"sectionnum\">Be sure that the <strong>Saturation</strong> setting of each color is about <strong>20-40%</strong> and the <strong>Value</strong> setting is about <strong>80-100%</strong>.</span></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"hue and value settings of the color\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35536/image/hue%20and%20value%20settings%20of%20the%20color.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 4</h3><p><span class=\"sectionnum\">Once you've found the colors you like, you can save them to your Creative Cloud library. Just select the existed library (or create a new one) and then press <strong>Save</strong>. Also, you can find </span>pastel color swatches for Photoshop to download for free in the <a href=\"https://color.adobe.com/explore\" target=\"_self\">Adobe Color</a> explore panel.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"Saving the color palette in creative cloud\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35536/image/Saving%20the%20color%20palette%20in%20creative%20cloud.jpg\"></figure><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">5.</span> Pastel Palette Photoshop Color Codes</h2><h3>Step 1</h3><p>Now I want to show you some very useful pastel color codes for your projects. Let's start with the Hex<strong> </strong>color codes: </p><ul>\n<li><code class=\"inline\">#f7959d</code></li>\n<li><code class=\"inline\">#f8b586</code></li>\n<li><code class=\"inline\">#f5f394</code></li>\n<li><code class=\"inline\">#d1f6b3</code></li>\n<li><code class=\"inline\">#b9cef0</code></li>\n<li><code class=\"inline\">#f3b6eb</code></li>\n</ul><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"hx color codes palette preview\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35536/image/Hex%20color%20codes%20preview.jpg\"></figure><p>You could play with the <strong>Hue</strong>, <strong>Saturation,</strong> and <strong>Brightness</strong> settings to change the look of the palette.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"changing the settings of the color\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35536/image/changing%20the%20settings%20of%20the%20color.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 2</h3><p>Let's look at the pastel color codes for the CMYK color mode:</p><ul>\n<li><strong>C=1 M=38 Y=0 K=0</strong></li>\n<li><strong>C=1 M=18 Y=0 K=0</strong></li>\n<li><strong>C=25 M=8 Y=0 K=0</strong></li>\n<li><strong>C=15 M=0 Y=2 K=0</strong></li>\n<li><strong>C=2 M=4 Y=8 K=0</strong></li>\n<li><strong>C=2 M=11 Y=18 K=0</strong></li>\n</ul><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"cmyk color scheme preview\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35536/image/cmyk%20color%20scheme%20preview.jpg\"></figure><h2>Conclusion</h2><p>Today we've discovered what pastel colors are and how to create pastel color palettes. Have fun with the color combinations, and show us your favorite pastel colors in the comments section! </p><p>If you are looking for pastel color swatches for Photoshop to download, then check out <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Envato Elements</a>, where you can find a really great number of high-quality Photoshop resources.</p><p>If you want to learn A  promotional flyer’s primary purpose is to attract attention. The secondary purpose is to convert sales—through information about unmissable offers or the details of an event, for example. </p><p>Sure, this means it’s not going to be a treasured work of art, but you can still make a flyer that looks incredible while fulfilling both purposes. These are important things to consider when thinking about how to create a good business flyer.</p>\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n<p>Read on to discover 15 professional tips for how to make a professional-looking flyer that makes the most of small print space and how best to attract attention from your target market. </p><h2>The Best Business Flyer Templates on Envato Elements (With Unlimited Use)</h2><p>You can find thousands of the <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/graphic-templates/print-templates/business+flyers\">best ideas for business flyers</a> on Envato Elements.
