Strongin</div></a></li>\n</ul><h2>Designing a Flyer: Top Tips for Professional Flyers</h2><p>Professional leaflet design inspiration can be exciting to look at. But what should a flyer include? How do we make it look great? Let's dig into some professional leaflet design tips, perfect for your next professional project:</p><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">1.</span> Function Before Form</h3><p>OK, so before we get distracted with the fun design stuff, let’s get a reality check first. You may want to make your new business flyer into a Michelangelo masterpiece, but realistically most people won't see it in that light at all.<br></p><p>Whether you’re advertising a computer sale or a club night, you need to remember that your new business flyer has to be striking enough to be picked up and looked at. This is a key part of how to make professional flyers. The information on it also has to be clear and concise enough to convince that person to check out your shop or attend your event. </p><p>You'll also need to consider questions like: </p><ul>\n<li>What should an info flyer include? </li>\n<li>What makes a good flyer? </li>\n<li>What does a professional flyer look like, in your experience? </li>\n<li>What makes an info flyer stand out? </li>\n</ul><p>The answers are all a part of how to design a flyer.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-consultant-flyer-8WYHARJ\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"How to Design A Good Business Flyer - Flyer Design Template\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_2b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>What software will you use for <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-consultant-flyer-8WYHARJ\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">your flyer design</a>? Templates like this one work in many software environments.</figcaption></figure><p>Prioritizing function over form before you start out designing will help to get your brain in the right place. Of course, design plays a significant role in converting sales. But it isn’t necessarily the most tastefully designed flyer that'll push the right buttons. </p><p>Take note of this functional checklist and review your new business flyer at the start and end of the design process to make sure it conforms to some or all of these. They're all part of how to make a good business flyer:</p><ul>\n<li>\n<strong>Keep the information concise. </strong>Edit the text content down to the essential information only, and don’t be tempted to waffle. The attention span of an info flyer reader is super-short, so make what they read in that split-second count. </li>\n<li>\n<strong>Make information easy to read</strong>. Make sure your font sizes are large and your leading generous. And don’t be afraid to let a big, bold header dominate a large part of the promotional flyer. This is one of the most important tips for making a flyer.</li>\n<li>\n<strong>Make contact details and other essential information instantly accessible</strong>. Pull out a website address in a bold color, or make sure the date and time of an event or sale is blown up to large scale.</li>\n<li>\n<strong>Apply a WYSIWYG (What You See Is What You Get) attitude</strong>. If you’re selling a product, make sure to feature an image of it. It might seem like simple common sense, but giving the reader a visual aspect to go with a text item will help your info flyer to convert sales much more easily. Take inspiration from this <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/products-sale-flyers/10771554\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">stylish sale flyer</a>. Each item of text is accompanied by a simple image of the product being sold. Treat your business flyer like a shop front. Shops put their products on display as they know that people ultimately buy with their eyes. When considering how to make a professional flyer, it makes good sense. We need strong visual associations with the objective.</li>\n</ul><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-template-AZGMY7K\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Business Flyer Template Design\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_8b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>A strong <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-template-AZGMY7K\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">business flyer design</a> is both visually engaging and functionally strong. Download this one today.</figcaption></figure><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">2.</span> Short on Space? Gridify!</h3><p>One of the biggest challenges faced by graphic designers is how to make a professional-looking flyer with a small amount of print space. With most flyers restricted to a standard <em>A5 (148 mm x 210 mm)</em> or <em>A6 (105 mm x 148 mm)</em> page size, you’re going to need to think a bit more creatively about how to lay out your design. <br></p><p>Whereas with an invitation or more formal brochure you might look to arrange text content into one column on the page, with a flyer you can and should be more experimental with your grid. Newspaper-style same-size columns might look a bit rigid, so try dividing your flyer into irregular sections. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-YEGQP6D\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Professional Business Flyer Design Layout\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_11b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Use a <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-YEGQP6D\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">grid-based flyer layout</a> to break up your layer in all kinds of interesting ways, like in this design.</figcaption></figure><p>The designer has created a four-part grid, with the top third devoted to the header and image, two irregular-width columns below, and a narrow full-width row at the base of the design. The professional leaflet design packs in a lot of content, but still retains a minimal, clean look thanks to the balanced proportions of the grid.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/multipurpose-business-flyer-G6U8QJ\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"How To Make A Business Flyer - Professional Leaflet Design\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_12b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Use a grid-based layout for a myriad of <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/multipurpose-business-flyer-G6U8QJ\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">creative flyer design</a> solutions. Download this design today.</figcaption></figure><p>Or why not move away from lateral thinking when it comes to how to make a professional flyer and try experimenting with diagonal sections on your grid? The <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/corporate-flyers/13736788\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">professional business flyer template</a> shown below breaks the normal rules with a diagonal slash across the top-right section of the flyer. It’s the perfect place for a slogan and background image, without intruding across the main layout. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/corporate-flyers/13736788\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Modern Corporate Flyer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/gr_fix_1b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>This <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/corporate-flyers/13736788\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">professional business flyer</a> uses a grid-based layout and employs some interesting geometry to complement it.</figcaption></figure><p>If you spend a bit of time at the start thinking of design considerations for a professional-looking flyer, mapping out your grid, and planning which content goes, where you’ll be amazed at how much you can actually fit onto a small page size.</p><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">3.</span> Play It Cool...</h3><p>Sometimes an understated flyer can be a perfectly pitched design move. If you’re aiming at the more intelligent or corporate consumer, it might not be the wisest idea to throw a rainbow of brights or a shouty novelty font into the mix.<br></p><p>Aim for an aesthetic that's minimal, subtle, and calm. These are the design elements of a good flyer. If you’re wondering how to design a flyer for advertising corporate services or a business convention, an understated, flat design style will attract your target market with very little effort.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/sanstemp-business-flyer-A3GZNE9\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Minimal Design Elements of a Good Flyer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_9b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Choose a clean, <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/sanstemp-business-flyer-A3GZNE9\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">minimal flyer design</a>, like this one, for your next flyer project.</figcaption></figure><p>Our graphic design tip for your flyers is to stick to a black, white, and grey palette. Restrict yourself to just one splash of bold (but appropriate) color. Teals, mustards, pale greys, and mint greens are corporate at their core and prevent the flyer from drifting into bland territory. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/corporate-flyer/12013641\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"How To Make a Business Flyer - Flat Flyer Design\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/gr_fix_2b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>This <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/corporate-flyer/12013641\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">flat flyer design</a> comes in three different color options, all employing the same idea.</figcaption></figure><p>Bringing in infographic-style icons and simple graphics will add a visual element without dominating the design. If you’re on the hunt for stylish icons, you can spend hours browsing the thousands of <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/graphics/icons\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">vector icons</a> from Envato Elements. There's also a huge selection of free-to-download vector graphics at <a href=\"https://www.flaticon.com/\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">flaticon.com</a>.<br></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-template-4724BX\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Minimal Flyer Design for Business\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_10b.jpg\"></a><figcaption> A <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-template-4724BX\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">strong flyer design</a> doesn't necessarily imagery. Keep things simple, like in this stylish design.</figcaption></figure><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">4.</span> ... But Don’t Be Dull!</h3><p>Whether you’re making an understatement or a full-blown statement, you want to avoid the curse of dullness at all costs. Transform understated designs from bland to brilliant with a deft application of color. Color is one of the easiest elements of a good flyer to apply.<br></p><p>If you’re looking to advertise something more informal and attention-seeking, like a club night, exhibition, or festival, you simply can’t afford to be dull at all! Great energy is what makes a good flyer.</p><p>You want to inject your flyer with the spirit of the event itself. Looking at your flyer should transport the viewer to the event and allow them to imagine what it would be like to experience it. If your leaflet is a little on the boring side and you don't know how to design a good flyer, they certainly aren’t going to get into the party spirit.</p><p>Follow these graphic design tips for flyers to make them more exciting and never be in fear of producing a dull design again:</p><ul><li>\n<strong>Color is your new best friend</strong>­. A palette of complementary bold tones, like the hot pink, sunny yellows, and sea blues used in this <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/photography-flyer/11363025\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">eye-catching photo flyer</a>, can conjure up summer days (perfect for festivals and BBQ events). On the other hand, a pop of neon can add a masculine, sporty edge to black-and-white designs. </li></ul><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/photography-flyer/11363025\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"How To Make A Successful Business Flyer - Colorful Flyer Design\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/gr_fix_5b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Check out this <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/photography-flyer/11363025\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">colorful flyer design</a>. It's playful, engaging, and memorable. Download it now.</figcaption></figure><ul><li>\n<strong>Balance a trio of bold elements</strong>. Create a balanced team of one striking photo, one attention-grabbing header (in a legible but bold slab typeface), and one colored element (such as the triangle pattern used on this <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/photography-flyer/11363025\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">photo flyer template</a>). Avoid overcrowding by sticking to this three-element rule. It’s pleasing to the eye and will be eye-catching without becoming an eyesore.</li></ul><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/fresh-startup-business-flyer-U8D6MHC\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"How To Make a Professional Flyer - Colorful Business Flyer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_16b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Color can make for a playful, energetic aesthetic. Check out this fun, <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/fresh-startup-business-flyer-U8D6MHC\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">colorful business flyer design</a>.</figcaption></figure><ul><li>\n<strong>Make your design optimistic and fun</strong>. Don’t allow the flyer to be too serious. Even if you want to bring in a corporate element, you’ve still got scope to make something look witty or even a bit childish. You want people to pick up your flyer and hang onto it. They’ll be more likely to do this if the design makes them feel good.</li></ul><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">5.</span> Bring Tech Appeal to Your Design</h3><p>Even though you’re probably designing your flyer for print, you may well be advertising services or products that can be accessed or bought online. More and more companies are moving their businesses solely online. As a result, most consumers interact with brands via websites or apps. <br></p><p>Flyers and apps have many things in common, even though a print flyer lacks the element of interactivity. Both flyers and apps are optimized for small spaces. As a result, they both need to make the way they present their information as efficient and easy-to-read as possible. They also are tasked with holding the attention of someone who may have many other distractions, whether that’s other apps on their phone or different flyers on a display stand. </p><p>Ultimately, apps are a great example of efficient, eye-catching design. If you're not sure how to make a business flyer, lift these lessons from the digital world and apply them to your print flyer designs. You'd be surprised by how the tech industry uses elements of a good flyer in their creations.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-6LDCCDK\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"How To Design A Flyer - Business Flyer Template Design\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_6b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Take inspiration from tech in your next <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-6LDCCDK\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">business flyer design</a>.</figcaption></figure><p>Look at some of the apps you most frequently use. What elements do they feature that would lend themselves well to print design? Whether that’s a strong, simple color palette, chunky buttons, or clean sans serif type, they’ll bring desirable and very modern app-inspired charm to your business flyer.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/corporate-business-flyer-98NXC54\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"How To Make A Good Flyer - Corporate Business Flyer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_3b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Note the tech inspiration in the icons—a design <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/corporate-business-flyer-98NXC54\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">like this flyer template</a> could be the perfect design solution.</figcaption></figure><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">6.</span> Be Approachable</h3><p>Nobody likes a grumpy face. You shouldn’t under-estimate the simple power of a smiling human face when it comes to learning how to make a professional-looking flyer. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/cuvac-business-flyer-hr-JBAJ2VM\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"flyer design template\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_13b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Consider working with a smile—as we see in this <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/cuvac-business-flyer-hr-JBAJ2VM\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">flyer design template</a>. Download it now.</figcaption></figure><p>For many people, a flyer is going to be their first point of contact with your business, so it’s vital to make a good impression. If you’re advertising services, it’s important to give the viewer a friendly face. When they do further research, even if that’s online or over the phone, they'll keep that person’s face in mind. </p><p>The otherwise minimal, restrained style of the flyer complements the image. It makes it look as if this man both knows what he’s doing and will be friendly and approachable in the process.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/creative-business-flyer-6ADPNTC\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Business Flyer Design\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_14b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Greet your customers with a smile—consider custom photos for <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/creative-business-flyer-6ADPNTC\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">your next business flyer design</a>.</figcaption></figure><p>A word of caution on using stock images—many stock photos of ‘smiling business people’ can look staged and soulless. Hiring a professional photographer to take high-quality, casual, authentic-looking photos of your business’s staff will be worth the money. Plus, the images can be reused for advertising, websites, or social media. </p><p>If your budget won’t stretch to that and you must use <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/photos\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">stock images</a>, aim for photos that feel casual, informal, and friendly. Browse a range of <a href=\"https://photodune.net/\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">high-quality stock images</a> over at Envato Elements and Envato Market.<br></p><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">7.</span> Don’t Compromise on Your Visuals </h3><p>It can seem a shame to restrict your photos or illustrations to just a small part of your flyer. But there’s no need to compromise with your design considerations for a professional-looking flyer! <br></p><p>You can turn striking photos into the main attraction by placing them behind other items of content, like text and color. Gradients and transparency effects are fantastic for allowing you to step outside the usual boxy grid layout and create a layered effect in your design.</p><p>These professional flyers let graphics and color take center-stage. But by reducing the opacity of the colored element and adding subtle gradients, the designer can make the text appear legible and stylish to boot.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/creative-business-flyer-LMVF9TY\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"colorful photo flyer design\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_18b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Color opacity can bring visual interest to your photos and your design, as in this <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/creative-business-flyer-LMVF9TY\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">business flyer design</a>.</figcaption></figure><p>When working with small page sizes, don’t feel limited to a basic grid layout. Layered designs can look particularly striking and are a surprisingly simple way of making flyers that look professionally designed.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-4HN3ZN\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"layered business flyer template design\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_19b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Layer colors and shapes to create different visual effects in your <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-4HN3ZN\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">business flyer layout design</a>.</figcaption></figure><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">8.</span> Use Shape to Create a Cool, Modular Design</h3><p>If you've got more than one image and can’t decide which one to choose, try experimenting with shape to create a modular style. A shape-based layout is perfect for creating a modern photo collage on your flyer, which is ideal for almost every kind of purpose where you’d like to showcase a range of products or images, from stock sites to retail brands.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/fashion-business-flyer-KJCU4VG\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"colorful flyer design template\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_4b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>This <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/fashion-business-flyer-KJCU4VG\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">stylish flyer design template</a> uses shapes to create interest. Add it to your collection today.</figcaption></figure><p>Shapes can add a lot of character and interest to your flyer design. This can create a number of different effects and suit many different aesthetics.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-template-CH7MPC8\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"business flyer design circles\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_7b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Playful use of shape can be a welcome addition to many <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-template-CH7MPC8\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">business flyer design</a> projects.</figcaption></figure><p>You can design an info flyer that takes advantage of a variety of shapes. This <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/promotional-flyer/11803268\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">promotional flyer</a> uses layered squares and rectangles, bordered by minimal white strokes, to showcase a range of product and fashion shots. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/promotional-flyer/11803268\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"promo flyer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/gr_fix_3b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>This <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/promotional-flyer/11803268\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Promotional Flyer Template</a> utilizes a variety of shapes in its layout design</figcaption></figure><p>Most software programs will have a range of default shape tools, including circles, squares, and polygons, which you can use to create a unique design. Learn how to use these programs while you figure out how to design a flyer.<br></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-8V6RZNH\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"How To Make a Professional Business Design - Abstract Shape Flyer Design\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_15b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Combine, create, and use unique shapes in <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-8V6RZNH\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">your business flyer design</a> to create visual interest.</figcaption></figure><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">9.</span> Tweak the Mood of Your Flyer With Color</h3><p>We’ve already touched on how vital a role color plays in making your flyer appear bolder. It really should be one of your design considerations for a professional-looking flyer. But where do you begin when it comes to selecting an effective color palette for your flyer design?<br></p><p>Color, arguably more so than typography or images, is the key player in defining the mood and personality of your flyer design. Color will play a significant part in enticing a reader to pick your flyer up. So you need to consider color as playing a strong psychological role in your design. </p><p>Citrus tones, like oranges and yellows, can appear zingy and optimistic, which is great for more informal flyer designs. Cooler tones like icy blues and pale greys can seem more intellectual and tech-forward, which is perfect if you’re looking to create something more corporate. Choosing an ill-judged color combination can alienate potential customers. But the right color palette can help your flyer translate to sales. </p><p>If you’re looking for a failsafe color combination that looks timeless and effortlessly elegant, I love the combination of black-and-white photography with a contrasting trio of complementary colors.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/photography-flyer/13462152\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"photo flyer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/gr_fix_4b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>This <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/photography-flyer/13462152\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">beautifully designed business flyer template</a> features skillful use of color.</figcaption></figure><p>Using black-and-white photography instead of full-color images keeps flyer designs restrained and makes a great backdrop for your brand colors. For added impact, choose bright neons or fresh pastels­­—teamed with monochrome photography, they’ll always look stylish, not garish. <br></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-template-K55S4T\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"creative flyer template\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_20b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Try color and overlays with monochrome photography, like this <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-template-K55S4T\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">creative flyer design</a>. Download it now.</figcaption></figure><h3>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">10.</span> Try to Make Your Flyer a Keeper</h3><p>Flyers are cheap to produce, often printed on low-weight paper with unfashionable gloss finishes. As a result, they're rarely seen as items to be treasured. They're the workhorse of promotional print items, but often end up in the trash. This makes it even more important to consider advertising tips for flyers.<br></p><p>A beautifully designed info flyer is much more likely to be kept by a potential customer. It may even be pinned up on display at home or at the office if it’s particularly attractive.</p><p>At the start of this article, we talked about the dual purpose of flyers—to attract enough attention to be picked up and to convert to sales quickly by presenting information in a clear, concise manner. But there’s another purpose—that of the long sell.</p><p>In a similar way to follow-up e-newsletters or online ads that follow you when you haven’t quite committed to a purchase, print flyers can be used as a long-term reminder to a consumer. This will only be a realistic aim if you’ve created a flyer that’s attractive enough to be kept around in view for a longer period of time. </p><p>If you treat your flyer like a mini-poster design, using striking images, beautiful colors, and stylish typography, it’s less likely to be thrown away as soon as it’s been picked up. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-A9ZSAVJ\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"business design flyer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_5b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>The <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-A9ZSAVJ\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">perfect business flyer design</a> will depend on our professional brand. </figcaption></figure><p>Don’t just think of the short-term role your flyer will have. Play the long game, and you’ll reap the rewards in the long term too with your professional flyer. Imagine this flyer design being pinned to a noticeboard or placed in a scrapbook for future reference. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/multipurpose-business-flyer-S2KABP\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"flyer design for business\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_17b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>There are so many ways you could take your <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/multipurpose-business-flyer-S2KABP\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">business flyer design</a>. Which will you choose?</figcaption></figure><p>Get more business flyer inspiration to help you find the perfect template: </p><ul class=\"roundup-block__contents posts--half-width roundup-block--list\"><li class=\"roundup-block__content\"><a class=\"roundup-block__content-link\" href=\"https://business.tutsplus.com/articles/20-business-flyer-templates-with-creative-layout-designs--cms-26171\"><img class=\"roundup-block__preview-image\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/23/posts/26171/preview_image/best-business-flyer-templates.jpg\"><div class=\"roundup-block__primary-category topic-business\">Marketing</div>\n<div class=\"roundup-block__content-title\">40+ Business Flyer Templates (Creative Layout Designs &amp; Industry-Specific Templates)</div>\n<div class=\"roundup-block__author\">Marc Schenker</div></a></li></ul><h2>5 Professional Business Flyer Design Trends for 2020</h2><p>Let's look at some flyer design trends. As you research and explore how to make a successful business flyer, it's a great idea to observe what works, what's timeless, and what's on trend. Learning how to make a good flyer is more than copying trends, of course. But visual research can prove to be valuable when developing the right solution for your professional flyer. <br></p><p>Consider these trends as flyer design tips: <em>observe, understand, and adapt to suit your professional brand.</em></p><h3><b>1. Typography With Emphasis</b></h3><p>There's a reason why it's trendy to use scale and color to bring emphasis to your type. It looks good, and it works well. That's why great fonts are consistently one of the top graphic design tips for flyers.</p><p>Where do your eyes go in the design below? Chances are, the red \"Dream\" really stands out. Why? The red commands our attention against the rest of the design elements. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-M5Z2JTJ\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Typographic Business Flyer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_trends_1b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Add emphasis and interest to your typography with scale and color, as in this <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-M5Z2JTJ\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">business flyer design template</a>.</figcaption></figure><p>Try this design trend with a sans serif type family. They tend to come with variants that make an aesthetic like this simple to achieve.<br></p><h3>2. Abstract Shapes as Design Elements</h3><p>Speaking of graphic design tips for flyers, this one will elevate the entire look. Abstract shapes can be a versatile way to add interest to your composition. They can also divide and organize your composition. In the example below, notice how the shapes serve many purposes. They highlight sections and influence the flow of the composition too.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-RBPZAJ\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Abstract Business Flyer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_trends_2b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>This <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-RBPZAJ\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">professional flyer design</a> from Envato Elements utilizes abstract shapes.</figcaption></figure><p>Abstract shapes don't necessarily have to be angular. Here we see curved shapes used with a different color scheme. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-WMZV2U\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Professional Flyer Design\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_trends_6b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Curved abstract shapes can be a smooth, organic addition to your <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-flyer-WMZV2U\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">professional flyer design</a>.</figcaption></figure><p>The nice thing about relying on shape as a design element is the versatility. Change colors, add imagery, and this approach can work for a wide variety of projects and subjects.<br></p><h3>3. Consistent Key Colors</h3><p>Color is very communicative. Consistent key colors are a trend you'll notice in many professional flyer design concepts. You'll see this in many flyer designs in 2020, as app-inspired aesthetics are often quite stylish. That sleek, tech-inspired look often benefits from consistent but limited colors.</p><p>Remember to make your color choices based on your professional branding. Color is communicative, too. These color choices should support your professional brand and its goals.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/yellow-business-flyer-P6LNFYB\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Professional Flyer Design\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_trends_3b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>This <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/yellow-business-flyer-P6LNFYB\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">business flyer design template</a> uses a single color, both for accents and for emphasis.</figcaption></figure><h3>4. Clean, Organized, Open Space</h3><p>Some design choices are timeless. Look at the examples below. Notice how there's generous \"breathing\" room. </p><p>The parts of the design visually relate to one another, but also leave a lot of open space—often called negative space in design theory. It can make a very classy and adaptable design. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/minimal-business-flyer-8BNDTHK\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Minimalist Business Flyer Design\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_trends_4b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Try out a stylish, <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/minimal-business-flyer-8BNDTHK\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">minimalist business flyer design</a>, like this one from Envato Elements.</figcaption></figure><p>For example, imagine the possibilities if you changed up the color choices and/or imagery. There's a reason why this aesthetic is still popular. It's because the versatility and professionalism can't be understated.<br></p><h3>5. Attention-Grabbing High Contrast</h3><p>What makes a good flyer? We want to create something attention-grabbing—and contrast is a great way to command attention. Contrast makes things stand out, while similarities in value make things more supplemental and complementary. You'll likely see this technique used regularly in 2020 as it's one of the top advertising tips for flyers.</p><p>Use this approach in a wide variety of ways. The concept below is a professional flyer that makes great use of this design concept.  Notice how the dark portions of the composition really stand out against the light portions.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/sanstemp-creative-business-flyer-UBLLW88\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"High Contrast Flyer Design\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/35085/image/business_flyer_trends_5b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Command attention and create emphasis with high contrast, as in this <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/sanstemp-creative-business-flyer-UBLLW88\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">professional flyer design</a>.</figcaption></figure><h2>Your Checklist to Make Awesome Business Flyers in 2020<br>\n</h2><p>In this article, we’ve looked at some top tips for how to make a good flyer—making your business flyers the best they can be. Keep this checklist at hand when you’re tackling a new flyer design project:</p><ul>\n<li>\n<strong>Consider function before form</strong>. Think about the practical purpose your flyer will play before you dive into the aesthetics.</li>\n<li>\n<strong>Apply an irregular grid</strong> to make the most of small print space.</li>\n<li>\n<strong>Consider an understated, restrained design</strong> for more corporate or formal businesses...</li>\n<li>\n<strong>... or make a bold statement</strong> with an attention-grabbing trio of bright color, strong photo, and bold typography.</li>\n<li>\n<strong>Introduce some tech appeal </strong>to your flyer with app-inspired design elements.</li>\n<li>\n<strong>Make your flyer appear friendly</strong> and approachable with personable, informal photography of employees.</li>\n<li>\n<strong>Make use of transparencies and gradients</strong> to create a layered effect without compromising on the impact of your chosen photography.</li>\n<li>\n<strong>Use shape tools to create a modular effect </strong>on your flyer—great for showcasing many images.</li>\n<li>\n<strong>Adjust the mood of your flyer</strong> in a flash by switching your color palette.</li>\n<li>\n<strong>Try to make your flyer a keeper</strong>. Convert more long-term sales by making your flyer into a beautiful keepsake.</li>\n</ul><h2>More Business Flyer Template Resources</h2><p>Looking for even more flyer design inspiration and design tips? Use this InDesign layout idea as-is, or you can easily add your own photos.</p><h2>5 Creative InDesign Layout Design Ideas</h2><p>In this section, we'll sample the best InDesign layout templates from Envato Elements. As you check out these designs, remember that all of them are included with your flat-rate subscription. They're easily customized and ready for your content.</p><h3>1. A Global Perspective</h3><p>In the King Julian brochure, the double-spread on pages 18 and 19 has a slick global map. It's perfect for a design that needs a worldwide perspective.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/king-julian-brochure-square-SE59UQ/preview\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Global Indesign Layout\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/151/posts/34076/image/sales-map-spread.jpg\"></a><figcaption>A premium global design like this one from <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/king-julian-brochure-square-SE59UQ/preview\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">King Julian</a> is a perfect creative layout design for worldwide teams.</figcaption></figure><p>Here are a few ideas for how you can use this beautiful, globalized slide:</p><ul>\n<li>\n<strong>Global locations </strong>for your company or organization, showing off the number of sites and offices you've got.</li>\n<li>\n<strong>Sources of raw materials </strong>that your company consumes.</li>\n<li>\n<strong>Employee locations</strong>, which is a perfect design for a \"work-from-home\" culture. </li>\n</ul><h3>2. A Flexible Flyer</h3><p>The best InDesign layout templates are flexible! That means that you can reuse them for extra editions or versions. <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/flyer-5TKRCK\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Flyer</a> from Elements fits the bill perfectly. Easy-to-use image placeholders make this easy to customize.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/flyer-5TKRCK\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Creative InDesign Flyer Layout\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/151/posts/34076/image/double-flyer.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Use a creative premium <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/flyer-5TKRCK\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Flyer</a> template for an easy-to-refresh, brief newsletter.</figcaption></figure><p>A flyer like this one would be perfect for a periodic update or newsletter. Departmental updates within your company are easy to create when you use a flyer template like this one.</p><h3>3. A Timeline Design</h3><p>Timelines are always a powerful storytelling tool. They're typically used to connect the past to the present, but you can also use them to predict the future. Slides 8 and 9 in <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/clean-modern-multipurpose-brochure-v2-3UAP3S\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Clean &amp; Modern Multipurpose Brochure V2</a> make for an excellent timeline.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/clean-modern-multipurpose-brochure-v2-3UAP3S\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Timeline Indesign Layout\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/151/posts/34076/image/timeline-indd.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Use a creative premium InDesign layout with a timeline to create a connected series of events.</figcaption></figure><p>Use a timeline to tell a story of \"how we got here,\" or chart the course into the future. Either way, using a beautiful creative InDesign layout like this makes it easy to create illustrative infographics. </p><h3>4. The Team Layout</h3><p>No matter what type of presentation or print-out you're creating, consider featuring your team. It builds camaraderie and a sense of recognition when your collaborators see themselves.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/king-julian-brochure-square-SE59UQ/preview\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Team Layout King Julian\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/151/posts/34076/image/crew.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Use a creative premium InDesign layout that features your team to recognize your peers.</figcaption></figure><p>The layout you see above in the <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/king-julian-brochure-square-SE59UQ\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">King Julian template</a> is excellent for showing the team members. It's perfectly split between two pages in a double spread. Just drop in <em>your </em>team's photos and descriptions.</p><h3>5. The Price Proposal</h3><p>Proposals help you put your \"best foot forward\" when presenting to a client. In the creative world, the packaging of the project matters just as much as your actual work. Use the template labeled <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/proposal-5Q4LHRF\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Proposal</a> for creative InDesign layouts while pitching.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/proposal-5Q4LHRF\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Price Proposal InDesign Layout\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/151/posts/34076/image/project-with-budget.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Use a premium budget template to lay out the pricing of your proposal.</figcaption></figure><p>Unfortunately, <em>so many </em>buying decisions come down to price. That's why you've got to meet the issue head-on when presenting to a potential client. This creative InDesign layout helps you lay out the budget to show the cost components effectively.</p><h2>How to Quickly Customize Creative Layouts in InDesign</h2><p>Found the perfect InDesign template, but not sure where to start? Whether you've decided to work with a premium template or you've found the perfect free find, your InDesign template is going to need the right adjustments.</p><p>We'll use this premium <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-card-B4KBRX\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">InDesign business card template</a> in this example walk-through. Download it if you'd like to follow along.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-card-B4KBRX\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"InDesign Business Card Template\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/34805/image/elements_sample_b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>This premium <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-card-B4KBRX\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">professional InDesign business card template</a> is available on Envato Elements.</figcaption></figure><p>Let's look at some helpful quick tips to get your InDesign template edited, customized, and ready for print in a snap:</p><h3>1. Edit Text in Adobe InDesign</h3><p>Working with type is an essential part of working in Abobe InDesign. Thankfully, doing so is simple. Select the <strong>Text Tool</strong>, as shown below, to get started.</p><p>In the case of this template, the goal is to edit text that's already been placed in the layout. With the Text Tool selected, simply click on the text box and then make your edits—it behaves much like standard word-processing software.</p><p>Prefer to add new text? Using the <strong>Text Tool</strong>, click and drag to draw a new text box. Then, place your text.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-card-B4KBRX\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Text Tool Adobe InDesign\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/34805/image/walkthrough_1.jpg\"></a></figure><h3>2. Use the Paragraph Panel in Adobe InDesign</h3><p>But you'll likely want to style your text too—rarely is text perfectly set to our liking, right out of the box! One way we can style our text is by using the <strong>Paragraph </strong>panel. Find it by looking under <strong>Window &gt; Type &amp; Tables &gt; Paragraph</strong>.</p><p>For example, in the example below, the text alignment has been changed to align right in the <strong>Paragraph </strong>panel.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-card-B4KBRX\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Paragraph Panel InDesign\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/34805/image/walkthrough_2.jpg\"></a></figure><h3>3. Change Fonts and Text Styles in InDesign</h3><p>But how about changing the font or the font size? We can do that in the <strong>Character </strong>panel. Not sure where to find it? Look under <strong>Window &gt; Type &amp; Tables &gt; Character</strong>.</p><p>In the example below, the name on the business card has been changed to a new font, Open Sans. We can change the style, too—in this case, Light has been selected. Change the size, the line height, and more in this panel.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-card-B4KBRX\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Character Panel InDesign\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/34805/image/walkthrough_3.jpg\"></a></figure><h3>4. Change Colors in Adobe InDesign</h3><p>Want to add or change colors in your design? There are multiple ways we can do this. One of the simplest is to select the <strong>Foreground Color</strong> in your <strong>Tools </strong>panel—note the small teal square in the example below. Click on this to open up your <strong>Color Picker</strong> and choose a new color.</p><p>We can also use our <strong>Swatches </strong>panel to choose colors that we've saved—or save a new color here to use it again later in your design process.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-card-B4KBRX\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Colors in Adobe InDesign\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/34805/image/walkthrough_4.jpg\"></a></figure><h3>5. Move and Arrange Your Layout Design in InDesign</h3><p>Moving and rearranging entire parts of your design is also simple—use the <strong>Move Tool</strong>. In the example below, the <strong>Move Tool </strong>is selected.</p><p>Select multiple parts of your design by holding down <strong>Shift</strong> while clicking, or click and drag while holding down <strong>Shift</strong>. Then, we can use the <strong>Move Tool</strong> to move multiple parts of the design at once.</p><p>Using the <strong>Move Tool </strong>is as simple as clicking and dragging with your mouse or using the arrow keys on your keyboard.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-card-B4KBRX\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><img alt=\"Adobe InDesign template\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/2092/posts/34805/image/walkthrough_5.jpg\"></a></figure><h2>Where to Find the Best Resume Templates in 2020 (Envato Elements vs. GraphicRiver)</h2><p>Premium templates definitely give you an advantage over free InDesign templates, which might not have as many features. </p><p>But there are plenty of great premium <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/graphic-templates/print-templates\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Adobe InDesign templates</a> out there. And finally, opt for bold and striking colors that'll instantly be associated with your very own fantasy team. What’s great about Placeit is that you don’t need fancy editing software to use the templates. Instead, all of the customization is done online. All you've got to do is make your changes in a web browser and click <strong>Download</strong>. The finished product will be ready for use as an image file. No need to worry with complicated and time-consuming edits after the download.</p><p>Let’s look at an example. For this, let’s use item #12 from above, the <a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/logos/stages/football-logo-maker-a245\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Football Logo Maker</a>.</p><h3>1. Open the Image<br>\n</h3><p>On each template, you’ll see a default icon and text. Each can be customized by using the menus on the left and right sides of the image preview.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"Placeit Logo Maker\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/151/posts/32220/image/Screenshot1.jpg\"></figure><h3>2. Replace the Text<br>\n</h3><p>To start out, insert your own team name by typing over the text in the placeholders on the left side. You can also change the fonts by clicking the dropdown menus.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"Placeit dropdown font menu\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/151/posts/32220/image/Screenshot2.jpg\"></figure><h3>3. Change the Colors<br>\n</h3><p>You can change the main and accent colors. These options are found on the right side of the image preview. Click each dropdown and select one of the pre-made color options by clicking on a box.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"Placeit change colors\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/151/posts/32220/image/Screenshot3.jpg\"></figure><p>Or, if you need total customization, click <strong>More</strong>. There, you’ll be able to choose a custom color from a color wheel or even input a color hex code.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"Placeit adapt color palette\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/151/posts/32220/image/Screenshot4.jpg\"></figure><p>This is great if you've got a designated color in a branding guide you need to maintain.</p><h3>4. Download Your Custom Fantasy Football Logo<br>\n</h3><p>When you’re done, just click <strong>Download </strong>right above the image preview. That’s it! Your custom fantasy football logo is ready for use. </p><p>The advantages of Placeit’s online editing tools really stand out here. Many sites require you to download a template and then make changes in third-party editing software. This is all fine for serious creatives, but casual users may not have the time or skill-set needed to use sophisticated apps like Photoshop. That’s where Placeit comes in. Anyone with a keyboard can easily make a one-of-a-kind, fully <a href=\"https://placeit.net/animated-logos\" target=\"_self\">custom logo</a> with just a few clicks. Notably, it can be done from any computer with internet access. There’s no need to install any other software applications to make the logos work.<br></p><p>Once you download the logo, you’ll have an image file that can be manipulated in a variety of applications. d178d466f747.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/151/posts/32220/image/Screenshot4.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx14/cdn49@2020_4/2020/08/24/23-59-43-006_26cda2811b0db2d2.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/151/posts/32220/image/ElementsScreenshot.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn45@2020_5/2020/08/24/23-59-45-907_7435ce05eccb894c.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/988/posts/32220/image/football-elements%20AB.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn71@2020_2/2020/08/24/23-59-48-994_e7ab6a8ebe602e8c.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/988/posts/32220/image/football-elements%20(2a).jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn80@2020_3/2020/08/24/23-59-51-844_b9ab3fe39a45e079.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/988/posts/32220/image/football-elements%20(3a).jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn9@2020_2/2020/08/24/23-59-44-291_782d19cd53f2a3f8.webp","http://audio.tutsplus.com.feedsportal.com/c/35227/f/668805/s/32220/sc/4/mf.gif":null,"http://da.feedsportal.com/r/186529796139/u/407/f/668805/c/35227/s/32220/a2.img":null,"http://pi.feedsportal.com/r/186529796139/u/407/f/668805/c/35227/s/32220/a2t.img":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn29@2020_3/2020/08/24/23-59-48-042_af4f302ed54618d8.jpg"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598313579864},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 07:59:39","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 07:59:39","title":"How to Make a Baseball Card Template in Photoshop","link":"https://design.tutsplus.com/tutorials/how-to-make-a-baseball-card-template-in-photoshop--cms-35513","description":"<figure class=\"final-product final-product--image\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35513/final_image/final-product.jpg\" alt=\"Final product image\"><!--googleoff: index--><figcaption>What You'll Be Creating</figcaption><!--googleon: index--></figure><p>In this tutorial, you will learn how to create a baseball card template in Photoshop. I will explain everything in so much detail that everyone can create the effect, even those who have just opened Photoshop for the first time.</p><h2>What You Will Learn in This Baseball Card Template Tutorial<br>\n</h2><ul>\n<li>How to design a baseball card Photoshop template</li>\n<li>How to create a sports template background</li>\n<li>How to create a star in Photoshop</li>\n<li>How to add text to a card design</li>\n<li>How to give text a border in Photoshop</li>\n</ul><h2>What You'll Need</h2><p>To recreate the design above, you will need the following resources:</p><ul>\n<li>\n<a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/young-black-girl-holding-baseball-and-mitt-looking-KCS3WME\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Stock Image</a>\n</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/lovely-kids-playful-font-JLUEM4N\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Font 1</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"https://fonts.google.com/specimen/Open+Sans\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Font 2</a></li>\n</ul><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">1.</span> How to Start Creating a Sports Card Photoshop Template</h2><p>In this section, we're going to start creating a sports card template. Go to <strong>File &gt; New</strong> and set the <strong>Width </strong>to <strong>2.5 in</strong>, <strong>Height </strong>to <strong>3.5 in</strong>, and <strong>Resolution </strong>to <strong>300 px/in</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating new baseball card template file\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35513/image/creating-new-file-2.jpg\"></figure><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">2.</span> How to Create a Template Border<br>\n</h2><p>Now we're going to create the template border.  Choose the <strong>Rounded Rectangle Tool</strong>, click anywhere inside the canvas to create a new rounded rectangle shape layer, and set the <strong>Width </strong>to <strong>730 px</strong>, <strong>Height</strong> to <strong>1030 px</strong>, and <strong>Radii </strong>to <strong>10 px</strong>. Then, set the <strong>Fill Solid Color</strong> to <code class=\"inline\">#ffe533</code> and center this layer both vertically and horizontally on the canvas. Name this layer <strong>Border</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating sports card template border\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35513/image/creating-rounded-rectangle-3.jpg\"></figure><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">3.</span> How to Create the Background<br>\n</h2><h3>Step 1<br>\n</h3><p>In this section, we're going to create a background for our baseball card template. Choose the <strong>Rounded Rectangle Tool</strong>, click anywhere inside the canvas to create a new rounded rectangle shape layer, and set the <strong>Width </strong>to <strong>690 px</strong>, <strong>Height</strong> to <strong>990 px</strong>, and <strong>Radii </strong>to <strong>20 px</strong>. Then, set the <strong>Fill Solid Color</strong> to <code class=\"inline\">#00a2ff</code> and align this layer both vertically and horizontally on the canvas. Name this layer <strong>Card Background</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating rounded rectangle\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35513/image/creating-rounded-rectangle-4.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 2</h3><p>Now choose the <strong>Custom Shape Tool</strong>, select the <strong>Registration Target 2</strong> shape, click anywhere inside the canvas to create a new custom shape layer, and set the <strong>Width</strong> and <strong>Height </strong>to <strong>1350 px</strong><strong></strong>. Then, set the <strong>Fill Solid Color</strong> to <code class=\"inline\">#ffffff</code>  and align this layer both vertically and horizontally on the canvas. </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating custom shape\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35513/image/creating-custom-shape-6.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 3</h3><p><strong>Control-click</strong> on the <strong>Card Background</strong> layer thumbnail to make a selection of this layer. Then, go to <strong>Layer &gt; Layer Mask &gt; Reveal Selection</strong> to add a layer mask that reveals the selected area of the layer.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adding layer mask\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35513/image/adding-layer-mask.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 4</h3><p>Now change the <strong>Opacity </strong>of this layer to<strong> 20%</strong> and name it <strong>Background Shape</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"changing opacity\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35513/image/changing-opacity.jpg\"></figure><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">4.</span> How to Add a Photo to the Baseball Card<br>\n</h2><h3>Step 1</h3><p>In this section, we're going to add a photo to the baseball card template. Choose the <strong>Custom Shape Tool</strong>, select the <strong>5 Point Star</strong> shape, click anywhere inside the canvas to create a new custom shape layer, and set the <strong>Width</strong> to <strong>625 px</strong> and <strong>Height </strong>to <strong>594 px</strong><strong></strong>. Then, set the<strong> Fill Solid Color</strong> to<strong> </strong><code class=\"inline\">#ffe533</code>, <strong>Stroke Solid Color</strong> to <code class=\"inline\">#ffffff</code>, and <strong>Stroke Width</strong> to <strong>10 px</strong>. After that, position this layer with the coordinates <strong>X: 375.50 px</strong> and <strong>Y: 435 px </strong>and<strong> </strong>name it <strong>Photo Background</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating custom shape\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35513/image/adjusting-shape.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 2</h3><p>Now go to <strong>File &gt; Open</strong>, select the<strong> </strong><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/young-black-girl-holding-baseball-and-mitt-looking-KCS3WME\" target=\"_self\">stock photo</a>, and click <strong>Open</strong>. Then, isolate the subject from the photo. You can follow <a href=\"https://design.tutsplus.com/articles/how-to-create-an-isolated-object-photoshop-in-60-seconds--cms-28867\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">How to Create an Isolated Object: Photoshop in 60 Seconds</a> to see how to create an isolated subject. After that, <strong>Right-click</strong> on the photo layer and choose <strong>Convert to Smart Object</strong>. <br></p><p>Using the <strong>Move Tool (V)</strong>, click and drag the subject layer to the baseball card template PSD file. Then, press <strong>Control-T</strong> on your keyboard to open the transform options and set the <strong>Width </strong>and <strong>Height</strong> of the layer to <strong>24%</strong>. After that, position the layer as shown below, and name it <strong>Photo.</strong></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"placing stock photo\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35513/image/placing-stock-photo.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 3</h3><p>Go to <strong>Layer &gt; Layer Mask &gt; Reveal All</strong> to add a layer mask that reveals the whole layer. Then, choose the <strong>Brush Tool (B)</strong>, pick a hard brush, and set the foreground color to <code class=\"inline\">#000000</code>. While the layer mask is selected, brush as shown below. Instead of brushing onto the layer mask, you can also make a selection and then fill it with a color.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adding layer mask\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35513/image/adding-layer-mask-2.jpg\"></figure><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">5.</span> How to Create the Stars</h2><h3>Step 1</h3><p>In this section, we're going to create the stars. Choose the <strong>Custom Shape Tool</strong>, select the <strong>5 Point Star</strong> shape, click anywhere inside the canvas to create a new custom shape layer, and set the <strong>Width</strong> to <strong>75 px</strong> and <strong>Height </strong>to<strong> 71 px</strong><strong></strong>. Then, set the<strong> Fill Solid Color </strong>to <strong></strong><code class=\"inline\">#ffffff</code> and position this layer with the coordinates <strong>X: 161.50 px</strong> and <strong>Y: 277.50 px</strong>. Name this layer <strong>Star_1</strong>. <strong><br></strong></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating custom shape\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35513/image/creating-custom-shape-7.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 2<br>\n</h3><p>Now repeat this process to add as many star layers as you want, and name the layers by sequence number. Feel free to use different size settings. Then, select your first star layer and <strong>Shift-click</strong> on your last star layer to select all layers between. Press<strong> Control-G</strong> on your keyboard to create a new group from the selected layers, and name it <strong>Stars</strong>.<br></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"repeating process\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35513/image/repeating-process.jpg\"></figure><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">6.</span> How to Add Text to a Card Design</h2><h3>Step 1</h3><p>In this section, we're going to add some text. Choose the <strong>Custom Shape Tool</strong>, select the <strong>Banner 4</strong> shape, click anywhere inside the canvas to create a new custom shape layer, and set the <strong>Width</strong> to <strong>545 px</strong> and <strong>Height </strong>to <strong>228 px</strong><strong></strong>. Then, set the<strong> Fill Solid Color</strong> to<strong> </strong><code class=\"inline\">#ffffff</code> and the <strong>Stroke Solid Color</strong> to <code class=\"inline\">#ffe533</code>. After that, position this layer with the coordinates <strong>X: 375.50 px</strong> and <strong>Y: 876 px </strong>and<strong> </strong>name it <strong>Banner</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating custom shape\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35513/image/creating-custom-shape-8.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 2</h3><p>Now choose the <strong>Horizontal Type Tool (T)</strong>, set the font to <strong>Lovely Kids</strong>, font size to <strong>80 px</strong>, alignment to<strong> Center</strong>, and color to <code class=\"inline\">#ffe533</code>. Then, click anywhere inside the canvas, type the text \"Baseball Team\" (or whatever text you want), and position this layer with the coordinates <strong>X: 376 px</strong> and <strong>Y: 861.50 px</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating text layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35513/image/creating-text-layer-6.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 3</h3><p><strong>Right-click</strong> on this layer and choose <strong>Blending Options</strong>. Then, select and check the <strong>Stroke</strong> style and use the settings below:<br></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adjusting blending options\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35513/image/adjusting-blending-options.jpg\"><figcaption>The color is #00a2ff.<br></figcaption></figure><h3>Step 4</h3><p>Now choose the <strong>Horizontal Type Tool (T)</strong>, and set the font to <strong>Open Sans</strong>, font style to <strong>SemiBold</strong>, font size to <strong>25 px</strong>, alignment to<strong> Center</strong>, and color to <code class=\"inline\">#00a2ff</code>. Then, in the <strong>Character</strong> panel, check the <strong>All Caps</strong> option and set the <strong>Tracking </strong>to <strong>200</strong>. Click anywhere inside the canvas, type the text \"Isabelle Silva\", and position this layer with the coordinates <strong>X: 376.15 px</strong> and <strong>Y: 923.57 px</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating text layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35513/image/creating-text-layer-7.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 5</h3><p>Choose the <strong>Custom Shape Tool</strong>, select the <strong>Banner 4</strong> shape, click anywhere inside the canvas to create a custom new shape layer, and set the <strong>Width</strong> and <strong>Height </strong>to <strong>80 px</strong><strong></strong>. Then, set the<strong> Fill Solid Color</strong> to<strong> </strong><code class=\"inline\">#ffffff</code> and <strong>Stroke Solid Color</strong> to <code class=\"inline\">#ffe533</code>. After that, position this layer with the coordinates <strong>X: 650 px</strong> and <strong>Y: 100 px </strong>and<strong> </strong>name it <strong>Background</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating custom shape\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35513/image/creating-ellipse-2.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 6</h3><p>Now choose the <strong>Horizontal Type Tool (T)</strong>, and set the font to <strong>Open Sans</strong>, font style to <strong>Bold</strong>, font size to <strong>30 px</strong>, alignment to<strong> Center</strong>, and color to <code class=\"inline\">#00a2ff</code>. Then, click anywhere inside the canvas and type the text \"CF\". After that, <strong>Control-click</strong> on the <strong>Background</strong> shape layer thumbnail to make a selection of this layer, choose the <strong>Move Tool (V)</strong>, and click on <strong>Align Vertical Center</strong> and <strong>Align Horizontal Center</strong> to align this layer both vertically and horizontally.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating text layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35513/image/creating-text-layer-8.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 7</h3><p>Select the <strong>Background</strong> shape layer and <strong>Control-click</strong> on the <strong>CF</strong> layer to select both layers at the same time. Then, press <strong>Control-G</strong> on your keyboard to create a new group from the selected layers and name it <strong>Position</strong>.<br></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating new group from layers\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35513/image/creating-new-group-from-layers.jpg\"></figure><h2>You Made It!</h2><p>Congratulations, you have \nsucceeded! You've learned how to create a baseball card PSD template. In this way, you can create any sports card template or any other sports templates.<br></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"final result\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35513/image/final-result.jpg\"></figure><p>Did you like this baseball card template Photoshop tutorial?
